Question #1 (ID: 237962)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Road Safety Awareness}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Road Safety Awareness}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Road safety is a major concern in Bangladesh. Every year, thousands of people die or get injured in road accidents. Most of these accidents can be avoided if people follow traffic rules and drive responsibly.[math]\textbf{Causes of Accidents:}[/math]
 The main causes of road accidents are reckless driving, speeding, overloading, unfit vehicles, drunk driving, and breaking traffic rules. Inexperienced drivers and poor road conditions also add to the problem.[math]\textbf{Importance of Awareness:}[/math]
 If people are aware, many lives can be saved. Wearing helmets, using seatbelts, not using phones while driving, and obeying traffic signals are basic safety rules. Pedestrians should also use footpaths and zebra crossings.[math]\textbf{Role of Government and Society:}[/math]
 The government should strictly punish traffic rule violators and ensure better road design. Schools should teach road safety. Awareness campaigns, TV ads, posters, and social media can spread safety messages.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Road safety is everyone’s responsibility. With awareness and discipline, accidents can be reduced. Let us all follow the rules and save lives.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it clearly defines road safety awareness, explains common causes of accidents, and presents practical preventive measures and a call to action within the 200-word limit. It follows a simple structure—introduction, body (causes and measures), and conclusion—so readers understand why rules like speed limits, seat belts, and pedestrian right-of-way matter. Understanding the underlying concept shows that awareness changes behavior and, combined with enforcement and safe infrastructure, significantly reduces accidents and saves lives.

Question #2 (ID: 237963)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Environmental Pollution}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Environmental Pollution}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Environmental pollution is one of the most serious problems in the modern world. It refers to the contamination of air, water, and land due to harmful human activities. Pollution is making the earth unsafe for living beings.[math]\textbf{Types of Pollution:}[/math]
 There are different types of pollution — air, water, soil, noise, and plastic pollution. Air pollution comes from vehicles and factories. Water pollution comes from industrial waste, oil spills, and garbage. Soil is polluted by chemicals and plastic. Noise from traffic and loudspeakers affects our hearing and mental health.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Pollution causes many diseases like asthma, cancer, and diarrhea. It destroys ecosystems, kills animals and fish, and damages crops. Climate change, global warming, and rising sea levels are results of pollution.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 We should plant more trees, use public transport, and recycle waste. Industries should use proper waste treatment. Plastic bags must be banned. People should be educated to care for the environment.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Pollution is a man-made disaster. If we do not act now, our future generations will suffer. Saving the environment is our duty.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it clearly defines environmental pollution and then logically covers its main types, major causes, harmful effects, and practical solutions within the 200-word limit, ensuring completeness and balance. It helps students understand the underlying concept by showing clear cause-and-effect links between human activities and pollution impacts on health, ecosystems, and the economy, and by presenting feasible prevention measures. Simple language, brief examples, and a concluding call to action make the ideas easy to follow and remember.

Question #3 (ID: 237964)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{A Journey by Train}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{A Journey by Train}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 A journey by train is an enjoyable and comfortable way to travel. It is safer and less expensive than other means. I had such a journey last year and it was one of the most memorable experiences of my life.[math]\textbf{Preparation:}[/math]
 During the summer vacation, I traveled from Dhaka to Chattogram by train with my family. We bought tickets two days before and reached the station early. The platform was busy with people, vendors, and announcements.[math]\textbf{Journey Begins:}[/math]
 The train started on time. I sat by the window. As it moved, I saw green fields, rivers, houses, and trees rushing past. The rhythmic sound of the wheels was like music. Vendors were selling tea, nuts, and fruits. We also brought food from home.[math]\textbf{Experience:}[/math]
 The journey was smooth. We talked, laughed, and played games. I read a storybook. The train stopped at many stations where new passengers got on. People were friendly and helpful. The beauty of the countryside made me feel happy and relaxed.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 After 7 hours, we reached Chattogram. It was a joyful and refreshing trip. A train journey gives us joy, comfort, and beautiful memories.

Explanation:
রচনাটি সঠিক কারণ এটি যাত্রার সূচনাপ্রসঙ্গ, ট্রেনে ঘটে থাকা ঘটনাবলি ও ব্যক্তিগত অনুভূতি ধারাবাহিকভাবে এবং সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে বর্ণনা করেছে, ফলে পাঠক সহজে দৃশ্য কল্পনা করতে পারে। এতে প্রাসঙ্গিক ইন্দ্রিয়বর্ণনা ও স্থান‑কাল উল্লেখ করে ঘটনার ধারা বজায় রাখা হয়েছে এবং পরিচিত শব্দভাণ্ডার ও পরিবর্তিত বাক্যগঠন রচনাকে প্রাণবন্ত করেছে। সংক্ষিপ্ত পরামর্শ: পরিপক্কতর করতে শুরুতে উদ্দেশ্য, মূল অংশে ঘটনাসমূহ ও ইন্দ্রিয়বর্ণনা, শেষে একটি সংক্ষিপ্ত উপসংহার রাখলে ২০০ শব্দের মধ্যে স্পষ্ট ও সম্পূর্ণ রচনা হয়।

Question #4 (ID: 237965)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Load Shedding}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Load Shedding}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Load shedding means the temporary stopping of electricity in different areas. It is a common problem in Bangladesh, especially during the summer. It creates serious problems in homes, schools, offices, and hospitals.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 The main cause is the shortage of electricity production. Other causes include misuse of electricity, old equipment, and poor management. When demand is more than supply, the authority cuts off power to manage the load.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Students cannot study properly. Business and industries face losses. Hospitals suffer during emergency treatments. Food gets spoiled. People sweat in the heat without fans or ACs. Internet and mobile networks also stop working.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 We should use electricity wisely. Government should invest in solar and wind power. Corruption and theft in the power sector must stop. Awareness programs can help people save power.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Load shedding is harmful for national progress. Everyone should help save electricity. Only then can we enjoy an uninterrupted life.

Explanation:
Load shedding বা বিদ্যুৎ বিভ্রাট হলো এমন পরিস্থিতি যখন বিদ্যুতের চাহিদা উৎপাদনের পরিমাণে বেশি হয়ে যায়, ফলে পরিকল্পিতভাবে বা জরুরি কারণে নির্দিষ্ট এলাকায় সরবরাহ বন্ধ করা হয়। দেশে বিদ্যুৎ ঘাটতি, জ্বালানি সংকট, অপর্যাপ্ত উৎপাদন সুবিধা, পুরানো ট্রান্সমিশন লাইন এবং প্রযুক্তিগত ত্রুটির মতো কারণে লোডশেডিং ঘটে। এর ফলে ঘরবাড়া, ব্যবসা প্রতিষ্ঠান, হাসপাতাল ও শিক্ষা প্রতিষ্ঠান প্রভাবিত হয়; শিল্প উৎপাদন কমে এবং দৈনন্দিন জীবন ব্যাহত হয়। ছোট ব্যবসায়ীরা আর্থিক ক্ষতির সম্মুখীন হয়, ছাত্রছাত্রীদের পড়াশোনা বিঘ্নিত হয় এবং রোগীদের জরুরি সেবায় ঝুঁকি বাড়ে। লোডশেডিং মোকাবিলায় সংরক্ষণ ও দক্ষতা বাড়ানো জরুরি — শক্তি সাশ্রয়ী যন্ত্রপাতি ব্যবহার, অনাবশ্যক ব্যাটারি ও লাইট বন্ধ রাখা, এবং শিল্পে শিফটিং প্ল্যান গ্রহণ করা যেতে পারে। দীর্ঘমেয়াদে বাড়তি উৎপাদন, গ্রিড আধুনিকীকরণ, নবায়নযোগ্য শক্তির উৎস বৃদ্ধি এবং জ্বালানি নিরাপত্তা নিশ্চিত করলে সমস্যা কমে। সরকার ও ব্যক্তি—উভয়ের সহায়তায় পরিকল্পিত বিনিয়োগ, সচেতনতা বৃদ্ধি এবং সাশ্রয়ী প্রযুক্তি গ্রহণ করলে লোডশেডিং নিয়ন্ত্রণ সম্ভব ও দেশের অর্থনীতি ও জনজীবন স্থিতিশীল রাখা যায়।

ব্যাখ্যা: এই রচনাটি লোডশেডিংয়ের সংজ্ঞা, কারণ, প্রভাব ও সমাধান সংক্ষেপে ব্যাখ্যা করেছে, তাই এটি বিষয়টি বোঝার জন্য যথেষ্ট ও সঠিক তথ্য প্রদান করে। শিক্ষার্থীরা এখানে সমস্যার মৌলিক কারণ ও প্রতিকার ধারণা সহজভাবে পাইবে।

Question #5 (ID: 237966)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Social Media}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Social Media}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Social media is a modern communication tool that allows people to share information, photos, and videos instantly. Facebook, YouTube, WhatsApp, Instagram, and Twitter are popular platforms. It has changed how people connect, learn, and express themselves.[math]\textbf{Advantages:}[/math]
 Social media helps us stay in touch with friends and family. Students use it for online learning. News spreads quickly. Businesses promote products. Creative people share art, music, and ideas globally.[math]\textbf{Disadvantages:}[/math]
 However, there are risks. Excessive use leads to addiction, depression, and poor sleep. False news spreads fast. People waste time. Personal data can be stolen. Children may face cyberbullying.[math]\textbf{Using Wisely:}[/math]
 We should use social media with caution. Set time limits. Verify information before sharing. Avoid harmful content. Parents should guide children’s use.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Social media is a powerful tool. It can help or harm, depending on how we use it. We must be smart users and use it for learning and positive change.

Explanation:
A correct 200-word composition is right because it fulfills the prompt by concisely defining social media, presenting its main benefits and drawbacks, and concluding while staying near the required length. Social media are online platforms for communication, content sharing, networking, and information spread, so the composition should explain these functions, give brief examples, and mention responsible use to show both utility and risks. Using a clear structure—short introduction, focused paragraphs on advantages and disadvantages with examples, and a concluding sentence—keeps the piece coherent, informative, and easy for students to understand.

Question #6 (ID: 237967)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Corruption in Society}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Corruption in Society}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Corruption is a serious disease in society. It means dishonest or illegal behavior, especially by powerful people like government officials, politicians, or businessmen. Corruption destroys the development of a nation, creates injustice, and spreads inequality.[math]\textbf{Forms of Corruption:}[/math]
 Bribery, nepotism, tax evasion, misuse of public funds, and cheating are common types of corruption. In many cases, people have to pay extra money to get jobs, licenses, or services that should be free or fair. It also happens in courts, police, hospitals, and schools.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 The main causes of corruption are greed, lack of transparency, weak law enforcement, political influence, and poverty. When people see that corrupt people are not punished, they lose faith in justice and become corrupt themselves.[math]\textbf{Effects on Society:}[/math]
 Corruption makes the rich richer and the poor poorer. It stops good people from getting opportunities. Roads, schools, and hospitals remain poor in quality because of fund theft. It leads to frustration, crime, and public anger. The whole society suffers.[math]\textbf{Ways to Stop Corruption:}[/math]
 Strong laws and punishments are needed. Digital systems and automation can reduce human contact and corruption. People must be educated to be honest. Media and civil society should raise their voice. Whistleblowers must be protected.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Corruption is a curse that destroys both individuals and nations. If we want a just and developed country, we must fight against corruption together. Honesty should be taught at home and school.

Explanation:
রচনাটি সঠিক কারণ এতে প্রথমে দুর্নীতির সংজ্ঞা দেওয়া হয়েছে, পরে লোভ, ক্ষমতার অপব্যবহার ও দুর্বল আইন-শাসনকে কারণ হিসেবে তুলে ধরা হয়েছে এবং সমাজ, অর্থনীতি ও ন্যায়বিচারে এর ক্ষতিকর প্রভাবগুলো স্পষ্টভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করা হয়েছে; শেষে শিক্ষা, স্বচ্ছতা ও কঠোর আইনগত ব্যবস্থা মতো বাস্তবসম্মত প্রতিকার দেয়া হয়েছে। এটি পরিচিতি, কারণ-প্রভাব, প্রতিকার ও উপসংহারে সুশৃঙ্খল গঠন অনুসরণ করে, যা বিষয়টিকে ধারাবাহিক ও বোধগম্য করে তোলে। সরল ও প্রাঞ্জল ভাষা ও প্রাসঙ্গিক উদাহরণ ব্যবহার করে রচনাটি ছাত্রদের দুর্নীতির মূল কারণ ও সমাধান বুঝতে সাহায্য করে।

Question #7 (ID: 237968)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Child Labour in Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Child Labour in Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Child labour is a serious social and economic problem in Bangladesh. It means engaging children in jobs that are harmful to their physical and mental growth. Millions of children in our country work in factories, hotels, shops, and households to support their families.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 The main causes of child labour are poverty, illiteracy, unemployment, and lack of awareness. Many parents are so poor that they send their children to work instead of sending them to school. Employers prefer children because they can be paid less and forced to work long hours.[math]\textbf{Types of Work:}[/math]
 Child labourers in Bangladesh work in garment factories, brickfields, tea stalls, and as domestic workers. Some even work in dangerous places like chemical industries and construction sites. They often face abuse, low wages, and health problems.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Child labour deprives children of education and a proper childhood. It keeps them in a cycle of poverty. They grow up with poor health, lack of skills, and low self-esteem. This creates an unskilled and weak future generation for the country.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 The government must enforce child labour laws strictly. Free and compulsory education must be ensured. Parents must be given support and jobs so that they don’t need to send their children to work. NGOs and media should create awareness.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Child labour is a national shame. Every child deserves education, care, and protection. We all must work together to eliminate child labour and build a better future for our children.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ২০০ শব্দের রচনা সঠিক হবে কারণ এতে শিশু শ্রমের সংজ্ঞা, বাংলাদেশে প্রাসঙ্গিকতা, কারণ ও প্রভাব এবং সমাধানগুলো সুশৃঙ্খলভাবে তুলে ধরে; এই ধারাবাহিকতা পড়কের কাছে বিষয়টি স্পষ্ট করে। রচনার কাঠামো রাখুন: সংক্ষিপ্ত পরিচিতি, প্রধান অনুচ্ছেদে কারণ ও পরিণতি উদাহরণসহ এবং শেষাংশে শিক্ষা, আইন ও সামাজিক উদ্যোগের মাধ্যমে সমাধানের সুস্পষ্ট প্রস্তাব; শব্দসীমানা মেনে প্রতিটি অংশ সংক্ষেপে রাখুন। সহজ ভাষা, যুক্তিসমপন্ন পয়েন্ট এবং সংযোগকারী শব্দ ব্যবহার করলে রচনা তথ্যপূর্ণ ও বোধ্য হবে।

Question #8 (ID: 237969)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Victory Day of Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Victory Day of Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 December 16 is the most glorious day in the history of Bangladesh. It is our Victory Day. On this day in 1971, we achieved our victory after a long and bloody war and became a free and independent country. It is a day of pride, celebration, and remembrance.[math]\textbf{Historical Background:}[/math]
 Bangladesh was a part of Pakistan known as East Pakistan. The people of this region were denied their rights and faced economic, cultural, and political discrimination. On March 26, 1971, the Liberation War began. Millions of people joined the war for freedom. After nine months of struggle and sacrifice, the Pakistani army surrendered on December 16, 1971.[math]\textbf{Celebration of the Day:}[/math]
 Every year, the nation celebrates Victory Day with great respect. The national flag is hoisted on all buildings. The day begins with paying tribute at the National Martyrs’ Memorial. Schools, colleges, and offices arrange cultural programs, rallies, and discussions. Newspapers and TV channels publish special content.[math]\textbf{Significance:}[/math]
 Victory Day reminds us of the sacrifices of three million martyrs and the bravery of our freedom fighters. It teaches us to love our country and stand against injustice. It also inspires new generations to protect independence and work for national progress.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Victory Day is more than a holiday. It is the heartbeat of our national identity. We must honour this day by becoming honest, responsible, and patriotic citizens.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it accurately describes the historical facts of Bangladesh’s Victory Day (December 16, 1971), highlights the sacrifices of freedom fighters, and explains the day’s national significance and celebrations in a clear, chronological way. It helps students understand the underlying concept by linking the historical events to their outcomes—independence, national pride, and ongoing remembrance—using simple language and a coherent structure. The piece is appropriate in length and focused content, making it easy for students to remember key facts and the emotional importance of the day.

Question #9 (ID: 237970)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Independence Day of Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Independence Day of Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 The 26th of March is observed as the Independence Day of Bangladesh. It marks the beginning of our Liberation War against West Pakistan in 1971. This day holds great importance in our history and reminds us of our struggle for freedom.[math]\textbf{Historical Importance:}[/math]
 On the night of March 25, 1971, the Pakistani military launched Operation Searchlight and brutally attacked innocent civilians in Dhaka. In response, the people of East Pakistan declared independence on March 26. Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman led this historic movement. The nine-month war finally ended with our victory on December 16, 1971.[math]\textbf{Celebration of the Day:}[/math]
 The day starts with the raising of the national flag. People gather at the National Martyrs’ Memorial to offer flowers and prayers. Schools and colleges hold rallies, speeches, and cultural programs. Special TV shows and newspaper supplements are published. Citizens remember the martyrs and freedom fighters.[math]\textbf{What We Learn:}[/math]
 Independence Day teaches us to value freedom and human rights. It reminds us to fight against injustice and protect democracy. The day encourages unity, courage, and patriotism.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Independence Day is a symbol of pride and sacrifice. We must protect our independence by working hard for a better, fairer, and stronger Bangladesh.

Explanation:
The Independence Day of Bangladesh is celebrated every year on 26 March to commemorate the nation’s declaration of independence in 1971. This day marks the beginning of a nine-month-long Liberation War against Pakistani rule, during which millions of Bangladeshis showed extraordinary courage and sacrifice to win freedom. The movement was led by Bangabandhu Sheikh Mujibur Rahman and supported by political leaders, freedom fighters, and ordinary citizens who arranged protests, strikes, and armed resistance. Throughout the war, countless people lost their lives, homes, and livelihoods, but their determination created the foundation for a sovereign state founded on the principles of democracy, secularism, and Bengali cultural identity. On Independence Day, nationwide ceremonies include hoisting the national flag, paying homage at the Shaheed Minar and Liberation War memorials, and organizing parades, cultural programs, and discussions that celebrate national unity and remember the martyrs. Schools, government offices, and communities participate in activities that teach younger generations about the historical significance and the values behind independence. The day is both a solemn remembrance of sacrifice and a joyful celebration of national achievement, reminding citizens to uphold the freedoms secured in 1971 and to work together for the country’s progress, peace, and prosperity.

Explanation: This composition is correct because it states the date, historical context, key leadership, and the significance of the Liberation War, while describing typical commemorations; these elements help students understand why the day is important and how it is observed.

Write a composition on [math]\textbf{A Rainy Day}[/math] in 200 words.

[math]\textbf{A Rainy Day}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 A rainy day is a day when the sky remains cloudy and it rains continuously or off and on. In Bangladesh, rainy days are very common during the monsoon. Though some people find it uncomfortable, a rainy day is a source of beauty and emotion for many.[math]\textbf{Nature’s Look:}[/math]
 On a rainy day, the whole sky remains overcast with clouds. The rain falls gently or heavily, depending on the weather. Trees and plants look fresh and green. Roads become muddy and slippery. Rivers, ponds, and canals overflow with water. Birds take shelter in trees, and the whole environment looks quiet and calm.[math]\textbf{Effect on Life:}[/math]
 For office goers and students, a rainy day can be troublesome. People get wet, buses run late, and traffic jams become worse. Schools sometimes remain closed. But for children and villagers, a rainy day brings fun. Children play in the rain and make paper boats. Farmers become happy as rain helps in cultivation.[math]\textbf{Food and Mood:}[/math]
 Many people enjoy hot tea, khichuri, eggs, and fried food on a rainy day. The sound of rain falling on tin roofs creates a peaceful feeling. Writers and poets often get inspiration on rainy days.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 A rainy day is a part of nature’s beauty. Though it creates some problems, it also brings joy, peace, and refreshment. It teaches us to pause and enjoy the simple moments of life.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it directly fulfills the prompt: it stays on the topic "A Rainy Day," uses vivid sensory details, and meets the required length. It follows a clear structure—brief introduction, descriptive body, and a concluding reflection—so the scene and emotions are easy to follow. To write similar compositions, plan main points, use concrete sensory words (sight, sound, smell), vary sentence length for rhythm, and keep paragraphs focused to maintain coherence and the word-count target.

[math]\textbf{A Visit to a Historical Place }[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Visiting historical places is always educational and exciting. It helps us connect with our past and understand our heritage. Last month, I had the opportunity to visit Lalbagh Fort, one of the most famous historical landmarks in Dhaka, Bangladesh.[math]\textbf{Location and History:}[/math]
 Lalbagh Fort is located in the old part of Dhaka city. It was built in 1678 during the Mughal period by Prince Muhammad Azam, the son of Emperor Aurangzeb. Though it was never completed, the fort remains a symbol of Mughal architecture and history. It holds stories of love, war, and incomplete dreams.[math]\textbf{What I Saw:}[/math]
 The fort is surrounded by high walls. Inside, there are several important buildings such as the Tomb of Pari Bibi, the mosque, and the audience hall. The gardens are beautifully maintained. The Mughal designs and carvings on the walls impressed me deeply. I also visited the museum that displays weapons, utensils, coins, and clothes of that era.[math]\textbf{Feelings and Realizations:}[/math]
 Walking through the fort, I felt like I had traveled back in time. It made me think about the lives of kings, queens, and common people during the Mughal rule. I realized how rich our culture and history are.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Visiting Lalbagh Fort was a memorable experience. It taught me a lot about architecture, culture, and the need to preserve our history. Every student should visit such places to learn beyond books.

Explanation:
The composition is effective because it opens with a brief introduction, gives vivid sensory descriptions and historical facts in the body, and ends with a personal reflection—this structure makes the visit clear and memorable while meeting the 200-word limit. The underlying concept is to combine factual information (dates, significance, architecture) with personal impressions and chronological order so readers both learn about the place and feel the experience. To write similar pieces, focus on specific details, clear sequence (arrival → exploration → reflection), and varied sentence length for smooth flow.

[math]\textbf{Mobile Phone}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 The mobile phone is one of the greatest inventions of modern science. It is a small portable device used for communication, but in today’s world, it has become much more than that. It is now a part of our daily life and a tool for work, learning, and entertainment.[math]\textbf{Uses:}[/math]
 People use mobile phones to make calls, send messages, take photos, browse the internet, and access social media. Students use it for online classes, reading e-books, watching tutorials, and attending virtual exams. Business people use it for emails, banking, and video conferencing. It has made life fast and efficient.[math]\textbf{Advantages:}[/math]
 Mobile phones keep us connected with others. In emergencies, it can save lives. GPS helps with navigation. Apps help in learning new languages, skills, or managing time. Online banking and shopping are now just a few taps away.[math]\textbf{Disadvantages:}[/math]
 However, mobile phones also have negative effects. Excessive use can cause eye strain, lack of concentration, and addiction. Students may waste time on games or social media. It can affect sleep and mental health. Some even become victims of cyberbullying or scams.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 The mobile phone is both a blessing and a curse. If used wisely, it can be a powerful tool. But misuse leads to harm. We should use mobile phones for useful and productive purposes.

Explanation:
Mobile phones have become indispensable tools in everyday life, transforming how we communicate, work, learn, and entertain ourselves. Initially designed for voice calls and simple text messages, modern smartphones combine computing power, high-resolution cameras, internet connectivity, and a vast array of applications that serve diverse needs. They enable instant communication through calls, messaging apps, and social media, while also providing navigation, banking, health monitoring, and educational resources. For students, mobile phones offer access to online libraries, video lectures, and collaborative platforms that support learning beyond the classroom. In the workplace, they facilitate remote work, virtual meetings, and quick information sharing, improving productivity and flexibility. Despite their many benefits, mobile phones pose challenges such as distraction, privacy risks, and overdependence; excessive use can harm concentration and mental health. Responsible usage, including setting time limits, using privacy settings, and choosing apps wisely, helps mitigate these problems. As technology advances, mobile phones continue to integrate with other devices and services, shaping smart homes, healthcare, and transportation. Overall, mobile phones are powerful tools that, when used thoughtfully, enhance convenience, access to information, and social connection, while requiring mindful habits to avoid negative effects.

This composition is correct because it briefly covers the phone’s evolution, main functions, benefits, drawbacks, and responsible use. It helps students understand the concept by highlighting practical uses and the need for balanced, responsible behavior.

Question #13 (ID: 237974)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Global Warming and Climate Change}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Global Warming and Climate Change}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Global warming and climate change are two of the most serious environmental issues in today’s world. Global warming refers to the rise in Earth’s average temperature due to the increase of greenhouse gases. Climate change includes global warming and its broader effects like droughts, floods, and sea-level rise.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 Burning fossil fuels (coal, gas, oil), deforestation, and industrial emissions are the major causes of global warming. These activities release carbon dioxide, methane, and other harmful gases that trap heat in the atmosphere. Cutting down trees reduces the Earth’s ability to absorb carbon dioxide.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 The Earth is getting hotter every year. Polar ice is melting, causing sea levels to rise. This leads to flooding in coastal areas. There are more droughts, heatwaves, and storms. Agriculture is being affected, and many species are becoming extinct. Bangladesh, being a low-lying country, is at high risk.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 We must reduce carbon emissions by using renewable energy like solar and wind power. Planting more trees, reducing plastic use, and recycling can help. Governments must take global steps, like following the Paris Agreement. People must also be aware and make eco-friendly choices.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Global warming is a threat to life on Earth. We must act now before it is too late. Protecting the environment is not only the duty of the government but also of every citizen.

Explanation:
A correct 200-word composition on Global Warming and Climate Change first defines the terms and explains the main causes—greenhouse gas emissions from burning fossil fuels, deforestation, and industrial activities—so readers grasp why global temperatures are rising. It then describes key impacts like sea-level rise, more frequent extreme weather, biodiversity loss, and health and economic harms to show the real-world consequences. Finally, it outlines practical mitigation and adaptation measures—renewable energy, energy efficiency, reforestation, climate policies, and individual actions—so the piece is balanced and solutions-oriented, which helps readers understand both the problem and what can be done.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Role of Technology in Education}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Role of Technology in Education}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Technology has changed the face of education. In today’s world, learning is no longer limited to books and classrooms. The use of computers, the internet, projectors, and mobile devices has made learning easier, faster, and more interesting.[math]\textbf{Benefits:}[/math]
 Technology allows students to access information anytime from anywhere. E-books, educational videos, and apps help students understand difficult topics easily. Online classes and virtual exams became common during the COVID-19 pandemic. Teachers use multimedia to explain lessons better.[math]\textbf{For Teachers and Institutions:}[/math]
 Teachers can prepare digital lessons, track students’ progress, and communicate through platforms like Google Classroom or Zoom. Schools use smart boards, attendance systems, and result management software. It saves time and improves efficiency.[math]\textbf{Challenges:}[/math]
 Some rural areas lack internet and digital devices. Students from poor families face difficulty buying phones or laptops. Too much screen time may also affect eyesight and attention span.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Technology has made education smarter and more accessible. To build a modern, knowledge-based society, we must use technology wisely and ensure equal access for all students.

Explanation:
Technology has transformed education by expanding access, improving engagement, and personalizing learning experiences. Digital tools such as educational software, online platforms, and interactive multimedia allow students to access information anytime and anywhere, breaking geographical and time barriers. Teachers use technology to create diverse instructional materials, assess learning in real time, and adapt lessons to meet individual needs. Adaptive learning systems analyze student performance and provide tailored practice, helping learners master concepts at their own pace. Collaboration tools enable peer learning and global connections, fostering communication and cultural awareness. Technology also prepares students for the modern workforce by developing digital literacy, problem-solving, and information-evaluation skills. However, effective integration requires thoughtful planning: equitable access must be addressed to prevent widening gaps, and teachers need training to use tools pedagogically rather than merely technically. Privacy and screen-time concerns demand clear policies and balanced approaches. When combined with sound teaching practices, technology enhances motivation and learning outcomes by making lessons more relevant, interactive, and student-centered. Ultimately, technology is a powerful means to support education, but its benefits depend on intentional use that aligns tools with curriculum goals, supports teachers, and ensures inclusion for all learners. Policymakers and communities must collaborate to sustain progress continually.

Explanation: This composition is correct because it succinctly covers the main roles of technology in education—access, personalization, engagement, teacher support, and workforce readiness—while also addressing challenges like equity, training, and privacy. The core concept is that technology enhances learning when integrated intentionally with sound pedagogy and equitable policies, not when used in isolation.

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Uses and Abuses of the Internet}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Uses and Abuses of the Internet}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 The Internet is one of the most powerful inventions of modern science. It connects people from all over the world in seconds. Today, it is used in education, communication, business, entertainment, health care, and almost every field of life. But like every tool, it has both good and bad sides.[math]\textbf{Uses:}[/math]
 The internet is a storehouse of knowledge. Students use it to learn, attend online classes, and access e-books and tutorials. People can send emails, attend video calls, and share documents instantly. Online banking, shopping, booking tickets, and paying bills have made life easier. Farmers get weather forecasts and market prices. Doctors use the internet for research and online consultations.[math]\textbf{Abuses:}[/math]
 However, the internet is often misused. Students sometimes spend hours on games, social media, or watching videos, neglecting studies. Addiction to Facebook, TikTok, or online gaming is harming the mental and physical health of youth. Cybercrime, hacking, identity theft, online fraud, and fake news are major concerns. Children can also be exposed to harmful content.[math]\textbf{Impact on Society:}[/math]
 While the internet connects people, it also isolates them. Family interactions are decreasing as everyone is busy on screens. Misinformation spreads quickly, causing panic and confusion. Online harassment and cyberbullying have increased. Internet scams cost people their money and trust.[math]\textbf{How to Use Wisely:}[/math]
 We must learn to use the internet carefully. Parental control and time limits can protect children. People should verify facts before sharing. Online etiquette and digital safety should be taught in schools.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 The internet is a blessing if used wisely and a curse if misused. It depends on us how we use it. Let us use the internet to grow, learn, and build a better future.

Explanation:
এই রচনা সঠিক কারণ এতে ইন্টারনেটের ইতিবাচক ব্যবহার (শিক্ষা, যোগাযোগ, তথ্যপ্রাপ্তি, ব্যবসা) ও নেতিবাচক অপব্যবহার (গোপনীয়তা লঙ্ঘন, অনলাইন প্রতারণা, অতিরিক্ত নির্ভরতা) সমানভাবে উল্লেখ করে নির্দিষ্ট উদাহরণ ও প্রতিরোধমূলক ব্যবস্থা দিয়েছে। রচনাটি সুসংগঠিত—প্রস্তাবনা, ব্যবহার ও অপব্যবহার আলাদা করে বিশ্লেষণ, এবং সংক্ষিপ্ত উপসংহার—তাই পাঠক সহজে মূল ধারণা বুঝতে পারে। ভাষা সরল ও তথ্যভিত্তিক হওয়ায় এটি ২০০ শব্দের মধ্যে প্রয়োজনীয় বিষয়গুলো স্পষ্টভাবে তুলে ধরে এবং শিক্ষার্থীদের জন্য পাঠ ও অনুশীলনে কার্যকর হবে।

Question #17 (ID: 237978)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Life of a Day Labourer}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Life of a Day Labourer}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 A day labourer is a person who earns his living by doing hard physical work on a daily basis. He works in fields, construction sites, factories, and markets. His life is full of struggle and uncertainty. Though his work is vital for society, his condition is often ignored.[math]\textbf{Daily Life:}[/math]
 A day labourer wakes up early in the morning and goes to the labor station or roadside to find work. Sometimes he gets hired; sometimes he returns home empty-handed. He works under the sun or in the rain. His work includes carrying bricks, digging, ploughing fields, or loading goods.[math]\textbf{Living Condition:}[/math]
 Most day labourers live in slums or poor huts. They often do not have access to clean water, electricity, or proper sanitation. Their meals are simple — rice, lentils, or leftover food. They cannot afford good clothes, education for their children, or medical treatment.[math]\textbf{Struggles:}[/math]
 A day labourer’s income is low and irregular. When he falls sick, he loses work and income. During off-seasons, disasters, or lockdowns, their situation becomes worse. Even with honest work, they are often treated without respect by others.[math]\textbf{Importance in Society:}[/math]
 Despite all these struggles, day labourers play a vital role in the development of the country. Roads, buildings, and crops would not exist without their hard work. They are the real builders of the nation.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 We must respect and support day labourers. Government and society should ensure fair wages, housing, healthcare, and education for their children. Their lives deserve dignity and better opportunities.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: প্রস্তাবিত ২০০ শব্দের রচনাটি শ্রমিকের দৈনন্দিন কর্মকাণ্ড, শারীরিক কষ্ট, আর্থ-সামাজিক অবস্থান ও মানসিক অনুভূতিগুলো সংক্ষেপে এবং বাস্তবতায় তুলে ধরে, তাই এটি সঠিক—কারণ জীবনচিত্র পূর্ণ ও ব্যাখ্যামূলক। রচনাটির সূচনা, মধ্যভাগ ও সমাপ্তি সুসংগঠিত হওয়ায় পাঠক ধারাবাহিকভাবে বিষয়টি মেনে নিতে পারে এবং সহানুভূতি জাগে। সংক্ষিপ্ত বর্ণনা ও উদাহরণের মাধ্যমে নিবন্ধটি প্রধান ধারনা—দৈনন্দিন সংগ্রাম, উপার্জনের অনিশ্চয়তা এবং মর্যাদা—স্পষ্টভাবে ব্যক্ত করে, যা শিক্ষার্থীদের বিষয়বস্তুকে গঠনগতভাবে বুঝতে সাহায্য করে।

Question #18 (ID: 237979)

Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Price Hike in Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Price Hike in Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Price hike means the continuous rise in the prices of daily necessities. In recent years, it has become a major problem in Bangladesh. It affects every class of people, especially the poor and middle-income families. The rising prices of food, fuel, and transportation are making life harder day by day.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 There are many reasons behind price hike. Some of them are natural disasters like floods or droughts that damage crops. Others include hoarding by dishonest traders, increased fuel prices, import taxes, transportation costs, and global market changes. Political instability and corruption also add to the problem.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Price hike creates great suffering. Poor people cannot afford proper food or medicine. Many families are forced to reduce meals or borrow money. Students drop out of school because of financial pressure. Crimes like theft and cheating increase when people become desperate.[math]\textbf{Impact on Society:}[/math]
 Price hike increases inequality. The rich get richer, but the poor get poorer. The middle class is disappearing. Social unrest, frustration, and protests become more common. It also damages trust in markets and government policies.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 The government must monitor markets regularly. Hoarders and corrupt traders should be punished. Subsidies should be given on food, medicine, and fuel. Encouraging local production and reducing dependency on imports will help stabilize prices.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Price hike is a threat to peace and development. It must be controlled with strong action, honest leadership, and public cooperation. Only then can people live with hope and dignity.

Question #19 (ID: 237980)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Food Adulteration}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Food Adulteration}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Food adulteration is a crime against health and humanity. It means mixing harmful chemicals or low-quality substances with food to increase quantity or shelf life. This has become a serious issue in Bangladesh, especially in cities and markets.[math]\textbf{Common Types:}[/math]
 Many foods are adulterated. Formalin is used in fish and fruits, calcium carbide in mangoes, textile dye in turmeric powder, and soap in sweets. Milk is mixed with water or detergent. These chemicals are highly toxic and dangerous for health.[math]\textbf{Reasons:}[/math]
 Dishonest traders do this to earn more money. Lack of proper monitoring and weak punishment also encourage this practice. People often cannot identify adulterated food, and there is no proper labeling system.[math]\textbf{Health Hazards:}[/math]
 Adulterated food causes cancer, kidney failure, diarrhea, ulcers, and even death. Children suffer from poor growth, and pregnant women face complications. Long-term consumption damages the body silently.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 The government must take strict action. Mobile courts, fines, and jail sentences must be applied regularly. People should be aware and check labels and sources. Scientific labs should test food samples. Media and schools should teach about food safety.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Food is life. Adulterating it is like poisoning society. We must say “no” to food adulteration and build a healthy nation with honesty and responsibility.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it clearly defines food adulteration and gives common examples and types, so readers understand what practices count as adulteration. It explains the health, economic and social consequences and outlines practical and legal prevention measures, which shows understanding of the underlying causes and solutions. The straightforward structure and simple language make the argument easy to follow and emphasize that consumer awareness, enforcement, and safe handling are essential to control adulteration.

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Drug Addiction: A Social Curse}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Drug Addiction: A Social Curse}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Drug addiction is one of the worst problems in modern society. It is destroying youth, families, and communities. It means the uncontrolled use of harmful substances like yaba, heroin, phensidyl, cannabis, and alcohol. In Bangladesh, drug addiction is spreading like a silent killer, especially among the young generation.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 There are many causes. Peer pressure, frustration, failure in education or love, lack of parental care, and unemployment push young people towards drugs. Smuggling from neighboring countries and weak law enforcement also worsen the situation.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Drug addiction ruins both body and mind. Addicts lose interest in study, work, and family. They become violent, depressed, or mentally unstable. Many die from overdose. Drug users often steal or commit crimes to buy drugs. Families are broken, and society becomes unsafe.[math]\textbf{How to Fight:}[/math]
 Awareness is the first step. Schools, parents, and media must educate youth about the danger of drugs. Strong border control and police action are necessary to stop smuggling. Addicts need love, counseling, and medical treatment to recover. NGOs and rehab centers must get more support.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Drug addiction is a curse that we must fight together. Saving our youth means saving the nation. Let us build a healthy, drug-free Bangladesh with care, education, and strict laws.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ২০০ শব্দের একটি রচনা "Drug Addiction: A Social Curse" তৈরির অনুরোধটি সঠিক কারণ এই দৈর্ঘ্যে বিষয়ের সংজ্ঞা, কারণ, সামাজিক ও স্বাস্থ্যগত প্রভাব এবং প্রতিরোধের উপায় সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করা যায়। রচনাটি হওয়া উচিত—সংক্ষিপ্ত ভূমিকা, মাদকাসক্তির কারণে ঘটে যাওয়া পারিবারিক-বৌদ্ধিক-অর্থনৈতিক ক্ষতি এবং সমাজ দেখা জরুরী সমস্যাগুলো, এবং শেষ অংশে শিক্ষা, আইন ও পরিবারিক সচেতনতার মাধ্যমে প্রতিরোধের প্রস্তাব; এমন নির্মাণ পাঠকের জন্য বিষয়টি পরিষ্কার করে। ভাষা সরল রাখুন, কারণ‑প্রভাবের সম্পর্ক স্পষ্টভাবে দেখান এবং শেষ করুন সমাধানমূলক আহ্বান দিয়ে, ফলে রচনা তথ্যবহুল ও প্রভাবশালী হবে।

Question #21 (ID: 237982)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Early Marriage: Causes and Prevention}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Early Marriage: Causes and Prevention}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Early marriage means getting married before reaching legal age. In Bangladesh, the legal age is 18 for girls and 21 for boys. But many children, especially girls, are forced into marriage at 14 or even younger. Early marriage is a violation of human rights and causes long-term damage to society.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 Poverty is a major cause. Poor families think marrying off daughters reduces financial burden. Lack of education is another reason. In many villages, people believe girls should marry early to maintain family honor. Fear of harassment or insecurity also leads to early marriage. Some parents are unaware of the legal and health risks.[math]\textbf{Negative Effects:}[/math]
 Early marriage ends a child’s education and future dreams. Child brides face health risks like early pregnancy and childbirth complications. Many suffer from malnutrition, depression, and domestic abuse. Their children also suffer from poor care and education. The cycle of poverty continues.[math]\textbf{How to Prevent:}[/math]
 Education is the best way to stop early marriage. If girls stay in school, they marry later and live better lives. Parents need awareness programs. Religious leaders and local authorities should speak against child marriage. The law must be enforced strictly, and violators must be punished.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Early marriage is harmful for individuals and the nation. It kills dreams, health, and opportunities. We must fight early marriage with education, awareness, and strict law. Let every child grow freely and safely.

Explanation:
Early marriage, the marriage of individuals below the legal or socially accepted age, harms young people and society. Causes include poverty, where families marry daughters early to reduce economic burden; lack of education and awareness about rights and health; strong cultural or religious traditions and social pressure to conform; gender inequality that values girls mainly as wives and mothers; and weak law enforcement that allows underage unions. Early marriage leads to interrupted education, limited job opportunities, teenage pregnancy with higher health risks, mental stress, and cycles of poverty.

Prevention requires a combination of legal, social, and educational measures. Enforcing minimum-age marriage laws and providing birth and marriage registration prevent illegal unions. Expanding access to quality education, especially for girls, and offering life-skills and reproductive-health information empower young people to make informed choices. Economic support for vulnerable families, such as conditional cash transfers or scholarships, reduces the financial motive for early marriage. Community engagement with religious and local leaders helps shift cultural norms, while media campaigns raise awareness about the harms of child marriage. Together, these steps protect children’s rights, improve health and education outcomes, and promote gender equality, creating a safer future for young people.

Question #22 (ID: 237983)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Unemployment Problem in Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Unemployment Problem in Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Unemployment means the condition of people who are willing to work but cannot find jobs. It is one of the major socio-economic problems in Bangladesh. Despite having a large population, the country cannot provide enough employment for its citizens.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 The main causes are overpopulation, lack of proper education, limited industries, and poor planning. Many students graduate with degrees that do not match market needs. Rural-urban migration also increases pressure on city jobs. Corruption and nepotism in recruitment worsen the problem.[math]\textbf{Types:}[/math]
 There are several types of unemployment — educated unemployment, seasonal unemployment, and disguised unemployment (where more people work than needed). Many young graduates remain jobless for years.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Unemployment causes frustration, depression, and sometimes crime. It increases poverty and weakens the economy. Skilled people leave the country, leading to brain drain. Families suffer from poor living standards.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 Technical education and vocational training should be encouraged. New industries and small businesses must be supported. The government should offer loans and incentives to young entrepreneurs. Corruption in job sectors must be stopped.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Unemployment is a threat to development. A nation cannot grow with unemployed youth. Creating job opportunities must be our top priority.

Explanation:
বাংলাদেশে বেকারত্ব একটি গম্ভীর সামাজিক ও অর্থনৈতিক সমস্যা যা দেশের সামগ্রিক উন্নয়নে বাধা সৃষ্টি করে। জনসংখ্যার দ্রুত বৃদ্ধি, কৃষিতে আধুনিকায়নের অভাব, শিল্প ও ব্যবসার পর্যাপ্ত প্রসারের অভাব এবং শিক্ষাব্যবস্থার দক্ষতা-অনুপযোগিতা বেকারত্বের মূল কারণ। গ্রাম থেকে শহরে সন্নিবেশ ও শিল্পায়নের তুলনামূলক দুর্বলতার ফলে শহরে কর্মসংস্থানের চাহিদা মেটাতে পারছে না, ফলে অশিক্ষিত ও আধা-শিক্ষিত যুবকরা কার্যত বেকার থাকছে। এছাড়া প্রযুক্তিগত দক্ষতার ঘাটতি ও প্রশিক্ষণের অনুপস্থিতি চাকরির যোগ্য জনশক্তিকে কর্মসংস্থানে বাধাগ্রস্ত করে। বেকারত্বের ফলশ্রুতিতে অপরাজনীতিক চাপ, দারিদ্র্য বৃদ্ধি, অপরাধ প্রবণতা এবং মানুষের মানসিক স্বাস্থ্য ক্ষতিগ্রস্ত হয়। সমস্যা সমাধানের জন্য দরকার দীর্ঘমেয়াদি পরিকল্পনা: গুণগত শিক্ষা ও কর্মসংস্থানমুখী প্রশিক্ষণ বাড়ানো, ক্ষুদ্র ও মাঝারি উদ্যোগ (SME) ও উৎপাদনশীল শিল্পে বিনিয়োগ বাড়ানো, কৃষির আধুনিকীকরণ এবং প্রযুক্তিনির্ভর দক্ষতা বিকাশে উদ্যোগ নেয়া। সরকার ও বেসরকারি খাতকে যৌথভাবে মেকানিক্যাল প্রশিক্ষণ কেন্দ্র, স্টার্টআপ উৎসাহ এবং গ্রামীন অর্থনীতিকে শক্তিশালী করার মাধ্যমে কর্মসংস্থানের সুযোগ সৃষ্টি করতে হবে। পরিবার পরিকল্পনা ও জনসংখ্যা নীতি কার্যকর করলে দীর্ঘমেয়াদে চাপ কমবে। সুনীতিপূর্ণ নীতি, দক্ষ মানবসম্পদ বিন্যাস এবং স্থায়ী বিনিয়োগের মাধ্যমে বেকারত্ব নিরসন সম্ভব।

ব্যাখ্যা: উপরের রচনাটি সমস্যা, কারণ, প্রভাব ও সমাধান সংক্ষেপে উপস্থাপন করেছে, যা একটি ভাল রচনা তৈরির মূল উপাদান। এটি মূল ধারণা — বেকারত্ব একটি বহুমাত্রিক সমস্যা যা শিক্ষা, দক্ষতা ও নীতি-উত্তর বিনিয়োগের সমন্বয় দ্বারা মোকাবেলা করা যায় — পরিষ্কারভাবে তুলে ধরে।

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Women Empowerment in Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Women Empowerment in Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Women empowerment means giving women the right to participate equally in all areas of life — education, employment, decision-making, and leadership. In Bangladesh, women’s status is improving, but still many challenges remain.[math]\textbf{Importance:}[/math]
 Empowered women contribute to family income, children’s education, and the country’s progress. They raise their voices against injustice and help build a more equal society. No nation can develop if half of its population is left behind.[math]\textbf{Progress in Bangladesh:}[/math]
 In recent years, Bangladesh has made good progress. Girls now go to school and do well in exams. Many women work in garments, banks, education, and even police and army. Women are now ministers, doctors, engineers, and entrepreneurs.[math]\textbf{Obstacles:}[/math]
 But problems still exist. Many girls face early marriage, domestic violence, and lack of safety. In rural areas, women often have less freedom. Social customs and lack of education make it hard for them to grow.[math]\textbf{How to Empower:}[/math]
 Education is key. Educated women become confident and independent. Laws must protect women’s rights. Workplaces must ensure safety and respect. Media and community leaders must promote positive role models.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Women empowerment is not a choice — it is a necessity. If we educate and support our girls, they will change the future of Bangladesh. Empowered women mean a strong nation.

Explanation:

It conveys the underlying concept that empowerment means increasing women’s agency, access to resources, education, economic opportunities, and legal rights, and it links these factors to concrete outcomes. This helps students by organizing key facts and examples logically, showing cause-and-effect, and suggesting realistic measures for further progress.

[math]\textbf{Traffic Jam in Dhaka City}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Traffic jam is a daily problem in Dhaka city. It wastes time, increases stress, and causes loss in economy. Millions of people get stuck on roads every day due to poor planning and lack of traffic control.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 There are many reasons. The number of vehicles is increasing rapidly, but roads remain narrow. Illegal parking, roadside markets, and lack of flyovers make it worse. Rickshaws, buses, cars, and CNGs fight for space. Poor traffic management and frequent violations of rules also add to the problem.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Traffic jam wastes valuable working hours. Students are late to school, and patients can’t reach hospitals in time. Fuel is wasted, and air pollution increases. People become tired and angry even before starting work.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 Public transport should be improved to reduce private cars. Metro rail and bus rapid transit systems must be expanded. Footpaths and cycle lanes should be created. Traffic police must be well-trained and strict. People should follow traffic rules and show patience.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Dhaka needs urgent action to solve traffic jams. Modern planning, discipline, and awareness can bring back smooth movement and reduce public suffering.

Explanation:
রচনা সঠিক কারণ এটি বিষয়ের প্রধান অংশগুলো—ঢাকার ট্রাফিক জ্যামের কারণ, এর দৈনন্দিন প্রভাব এবং সম্ভাব্য সমাধান—সংগঠিতভাবে ও সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে তুলে ধরেছে। ভাষা সহজ হওয়ায় শিক্ষার্থীরা সহজে বুঝবে এবং ধারাবাহিকতা বজায় থাকায় তথ্যের সম্পর্ক স্পষ্ট হবে। এছাড়া রচনাটি নির্দিষ্ট শব্দসীমা মেনে ভূমিকা, প্রধান অংশ ও উপসংহার উল্লেখ করেছে, ফলে বিষয়টি সম্পূর্ণভাবে বোঝা যায়।

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Deforestation and Its Effects}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Deforestation and Its Effects}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Deforestation means cutting down trees and destroying forests. It is one of the biggest threats to nature and human survival. In Bangladesh, forests are disappearing rapidly due to overpopulation, urbanization, and industrial needs.[math]\textbf{Causes:}[/math]
 People cut trees for fuel, farming, furniture, and construction. Forests are cleared for roads, buildings, and factories. Illegal logging and forest fires also cause destruction. Many don’t realize the long-term effects.[math]\textbf{Effects:}[/math]
 Deforestation leads to soil erosion, loss of wildlife, and climate change. It reduces rainfall and increases temperature. Rivers dry up, and natural disasters like floods and droughts become common. Animals lose their homes, and biodiversity is damaged. It also affects air quality and health.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 We must plant trees regularly. Deforested lands should be reforested. Alternative fuels should be used to reduce tree cutting. Forest laws must be enforced strictly. People should be educated on the value of trees.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Trees are our natural friends. If forests die, life on Earth will become impossible. We must protect forests for ourselves and future generations. Deforestation must stop now.

Explanation:
এই রচনাটি সঠিক কারণ এতে 'ডিফরেস্টেশন' বা বন উজাড়ের সংজ্ঞা ও প্রধান কারণগুলো স্পষ্টভাবে তুলে ধরা হয়েছে। এতে বন উজাড়ের ফলসমূহ—জলবায়ু পরিবর্তন, জীববৈচিত্র্য হ্রাস, মাটি ক্ষয় ও জলের চক্রে বিঘ্ন—কারণ-প্রভাবের সঙ্গে সংক্ষেপে ব্যাখ্যা করা হয়েছে, যা মূল ধারণা বোঝাতে সাহায্য করে। পাশাপাশি প্রতিরোধমূলক ব্যবস্থা ও সমাধান উল্লেখ করে রচনাটি শিক্ষামূলক, সুসংগঠিত এবং নির্দিষ্ট শব্দসীমার মধ্যে উপস্থাপন করা হয়েছে।

Question #26 (ID: 237987)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Gender Equality in Education}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Gender Equality in Education}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Gender equality in education means giving boys and girls equal rights and opportunities to study, grow, and succeed. In many parts of the world, especially in developing countries like Bangladesh, girls have historically faced more challenges in accessing education. But without gender equality, true development is not possible.[math]\textbf{Why It Matters:}[/math]
 When girls are educated, they become healthier, economically stronger, and more confident. They can support their families, raise better-educated children, and take leadership roles in society. Boys and girls must be treated equally in schools, colleges, and society. Education is a right, not a privilege based on gender.[math]\textbf{Current Situation in Bangladesh:}[/math]
 In recent years, Bangladesh has made progress. Girls now outnumber boys in many schools. Government programs like stipends and free books have helped improve girls’ attendance. Female teachers are encouraged, and awareness is rising. However, in rural areas, early marriage, poverty, and family restrictions still prevent many girls from continuing their education.[math]\textbf{Challenges:}[/math]
 Girls often face harassment on the way to school, lack of toilets, and unsafe environments. Some families still believe that girls do not need higher education. These social attitudes must change.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 More schools should be built closer to homes. Safety must be ensured. Parents need awareness. Laws against early marriage and gender discrimination should be strictly enforced. Both boys and girls should learn to respect each other.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Gender equality in education is essential for a fair, successful, and developed society. Let us ensure every child, regardless of gender, gets equal chance to learn and lead.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: লেখাটি লিঙ্গ সমতার মূল ধারণা, শিক্ষার সামাজিক ও অর্থনৈতিক গুরুত্ব, এবং বাল্যবিবাহ ও বৈষম্যের মতো বাধাগুলোকে সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে তুলে ধরে। এটি প্রতিটি অনুচ্ছেদে একটি প্রধান ধারণা ও উদাহরণ দিয়ে বিন্যস্ত—থিসিস, সমর্থন ও সমাধান—যা পাঠককে বিষয়টি সহজে বুঝতে সাহায্য করে। ফলে রচনাটি প্রয়োজনীয় তথ্য, কারণ ও বাস্তব কর্মপরিকল্পনা দিয়ে শিক্ষায় লিঙ্গ সমতার গুরুত্ব স্পষ্টভাবে প্রতিষ্ঠা করে।

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Padma Bridge: A Symbol of National Pride}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Padma Bridge: A Symbol of National Pride}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 The Padma Bridge is one of the most remarkable achievements in the history of Bangladesh. It stands as a symbol of national pride, strength, and self-reliance. After many challenges and delays, it was finally opened to the public on June 25, 2022. This bridge has connected the southern part of Bangladesh with the capital and northern districts.[math]\textbf{Construction and Significance:}[/math]
 The Padma Bridge is the largest bridge ever built in Bangladesh. It is a multipurpose road-rail bridge, 6.15 kilometers long. It was constructed with the country’s own funding, without foreign aid, which makes it even more special. It shows Bangladesh’s determination to overcome challenges.[math]\textbf{Benefits:}[/math]
 This bridge will boost trade, travel, and communication. It will reduce travel time and cost for people living in the southern districts. It will also improve healthcare, education, and business in those areas. Farmers and entrepreneurs can now reach markets faster. The bridge is expected to increase the national GDP by more than 1% in the coming years.[math]\textbf{Symbolic Value:}[/math]
 Beyond practical benefits, the Padma Bridge is a source of pride. It proves that Bangladesh can take on mega projects with its own talent and resources. It is a gift of courage, vision, and engineering brilliance.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 The Padma Bridge is not just a structure — it is a symbol of unity and progress. It reminds us what a nation can achieve with strong will and hard work. Every citizen of Bangladesh feels proud of it.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it directly addresses the prompt—portraying the Padma Bridge as a symbol of national pride—by describing its engineering achievement, economic and social benefits, and the unity behind its construction while keeping within the 200-word requirement. The underlying concept is to organize ideas into a clear introduction, supporting paragraphs that use concrete facts and emotional appeal (construction feat, connectivity, development), and a concise conclusion that reinforces the bridge’s symbolic meaning. For students: focus on a logical structure, include specific impacts and a brief historical or technical note, use simple language and varied sentences, and monitor word count to meet the 200-word target.

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Importance of Reading Books}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Books are called the best friends of human beings. They are a great source of knowledge, entertainment, and wisdom. Reading books develops our personality, improves language skills, and helps us understand life better. In this digital age, reading is more important than ever.[math]\textbf{Benefits of Reading:}[/math]
 Reading increases vocabulary and improves communication skills. It enhances imagination and creativity. Books inspire people, motivate them, and change their mindset. Reading also reduces stress, improves memory, and sharpens the brain.[math]\textbf{Types of Books:}[/math]
 Different people enjoy different kinds of books — story books, novels, biographies, science books, religious books, and history books. Each type helps us grow in different ways. Fiction teaches empathy and culture; non-fiction teaches facts and life skills.[math]\textbf{Role in Student Life:}[/math]
 For students, reading is the foundation of learning. Good books shape young minds. They prepare students to face challenges and become responsible citizens. Textbooks help in exams, but extra reading builds confidence and curiosity.[math]\textbf{Reading Habit:}[/math]
 Unfortunately, many students today spend more time on phones than books. Libraries should be improved and reading clubs introduced. Parents and teachers should encourage reading from childhood.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Reading books is a lifelong gift. It opens doors to knowledge and new worlds. Everyone should read regularly and make books their true companions.

Explanation:

The underlying concept is to organize ideas clearly (short introduction, 2–3 supporting paragraphs with concrete examples or benefits, and a brief conclusion) and use simple, coherent sentences and linking words so each point follows logically. To meet the task, prioritize the strongest points, give one or two specific examples, and watch word-choice and sentence length to stay within the 200-word limit.

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Role of Youth in National Development}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Youth are the strength and future of a nation. They are energetic, creative, and full of new ideas. If guided properly, they can lead a country towards prosperity and progress. In Bangladesh, a large portion of the population is young. Therefore, the role of youth in national development is very crucial.[math]\textbf{Contribution in Education and Innovation:}[/math]
 Educated and skilled youth bring innovation to technology, science, and business. They research, invent, and improve processes. Young people can solve national problems like unemployment, corruption, and poverty through new ideas and entrepreneurship.[math]\textbf{Social and Political Engagement:}[/math]

In politics, honest and educated youth can promote transparency and ethical leadership.[math]\textbf{Economic Development:}[/math]
 Young entrepreneurs start small businesses and create jobs. Skilled workers in ICT, freelancing, and startups are earning foreign currency. Agriculture and rural development also benefit from youth involvement with modern tools and methods.[math]\textbf{Obstacles and Solutions:}[/math]

রচনা সঠিক কারণ এতে যুবসমাজের মূল ভূমিকা—শিক্ষা ও দক্ষতা অর্জন, উদ্ভাবন ও উদ্যোক্তা মনোভাব, নেতৃত্ব ও নাগরিক অংশগ্রহণ—স্পষ্টভাবে তুলেধরা হয়েছে এবং এসব দিক কীভাবে অর্থনৈতিক ও সামাজিক উন্নয়নে যোগান দেয় তা সংযোজিত হয়েছে। মূল ধারণাটি হলো: যুবরা হলো দেশের মানবসম্পদ; তাদের জ্ঞান, শক্তি ও সৃজনশীলতাই কর্মসংস্থান, প্রযুক্তিগত অগ্রগতি ও সামাজিক পরিবর্তন ত্বরান্বিত করে। তাই রচনায় যুবদের দায়িত্ব ও নীতিগত সহায়তার (শিক্ষা, কর্মসংস্থান, সুযোগ) প্রয়োজনীয়তাও উল্লেখ করলে বিষয়টি পূর্ণতা পায়।

Question #31 (ID: 237992)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Impact of COVID-19 on Education}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Impact of COVID-19 on Education}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 The COVID-19 pandemic affected every part of life across the world. One of the sectors hit hardest was education. Schools, colleges, and universities were closed for months. Students, teachers, and parents faced an entirely new way of learning. In Bangladesh, the impact was even more serious because of limited digital access.[math]\textbf{Closure of Institutions:}[/math]
 Educational institutions were closed for over a year. Board exams were delayed or canceled. Millions of students lost connection with formal learning. Children in rural areas suffered the most due to lack of smartphones, internet, or even electricity.[math]\textbf{Online Education:}[/math]
 During the pandemic, online classes became the new normal. Platforms like Zoom, Google Meet, and YouTube were used. However, not all students could attend regularly. Network issues, lack of devices, and poor digital literacy were common problems. Many students lost interest and motivation.[math]\textbf{Mental Health and Social Impact:}[/math]
 Isolation from classmates, stress of online learning, and uncertainty about exams caused mental pressure. Many students fell into depression, anxiety, or laziness. Physical activities stopped, and social development was hampered.[math]\textbf{Positive Outcomes:}[/math]
 Despite challenges, the crisis increased awareness of digital learning. Teachers and students learned new technologies. Educational apps and TV programs (like Sangsad TV in Bangladesh) reached some remote learners. It also showed the importance of internet and IT in education.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 COVID-19 showed us that education must be flexible and accessible to all. Digital tools must be developed, and students must be supported emotionally and technologically. Education must go on, no matter the situation.

Explanation:
The COVID-19 pandemic transformed education worldwide, forcing schools and universities to close and shifting learning from classrooms to homes. Remote learning and online platforms became essential, revealing both strengths and weaknesses of education systems. While technology enabled continuity of instruction for many students, lack of access to devices, reliable internet and digital skills widened existing inequalities. Teachers adapted quickly, redesigning lessons and using new tools, but many faced heavy workloads and limited training. Students experienced disruptions in learning progress, reduced social interaction, and increased stress, leading to concerns about long-term learning loss and well-being. Assessment and examinations required major adjustments to ensure fairness and validity. At the same time, the crisis accelerated innovation: schools expanded digital resources, blended learning models gained acceptance, and policymakers invested in infrastructure and teacher development. Community and family involvement in education increased as parents supported home learning. Recovery efforts focus on targeted remedial programs, mental health support, and measures to close equity gaps. In sum, COVID-19 exposed vulnerabilities in education systems but also created opportunities to innovate, strengthen resilience, and promote more inclusive, flexible approaches to teaching and learning in the future. Global collaboration and sustained funding are vital to secure these gains and equity.

Explanation: This composition highlights the main impacts—disruption, digital divide, teacher and student challenges—and responses like innovation and recovery, showing cause and effect. It helps students grasp both the problems COVID-19 created for education and the measures needed to build more resilient, equitable systems.

Question #32 (ID: 237993)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Renewable Energy for a Sustainable Future}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Renewable Energy for a Sustainable Future}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Renewable energy means energy from natural sources like the sun, wind, water, and biomass that do not run out. It is clean, safe, and environmentally friendly. In the face of climate change and energy crisis, renewable energy is the only path to a sustainable and secure future.[math]\textbf{Types of Renewable Energy:}[/math]
 The main types are solar energy, wind energy, hydroelectric power, geothermal energy, and biomass energy. These sources are naturally replenished and do not pollute the environment. Solar panels collect sunlight, wind turbines use wind, and dams produce electricity from flowing water.[math]\textbf{Importance:}[/math]
 Fossil fuels like coal and oil are limited and harmful to the environment. They cause pollution, global warming, and health issues. Renewable energy reduces carbon emissions, slows down climate change, and keeps the air clean. It also creates green jobs and makes countries energy-independent.[math]\textbf{Renewable Energy in Bangladesh:}[/math]
 Bangladesh has good potential for solar and wind energy. Many schools and homes in rural areas now use solar panels. The government is promoting “Green Energy” through different projects. Off-grid solar systems have brought electricity to remote villages.[math]\textbf{Challenges:}[/math]
 High initial costs, lack of technology, and lack of skilled manpower are the main barriers. People also lack awareness of the long-term benefits. More investment, training, and research are needed.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Renewable energy is not just a choice — it is a necessity. For a clean, healthy, and sustainable world, we must shift from fossil fuels to renewable sources. Every step toward green energy is a step toward saving the planet.

Explanation:
Renewable energy sources—such as solar, wind, hydro, geothermal, and biomass—offer clean, abundant alternatives to fossil fuels and are essential for a sustainable future. By harnessing natural processes that are continually replenished, renewable technologies reduce greenhouse gas emissions, improve air quality, and lessen dependence on finite resources. Widespread adoption stimulates technological innovation, creates green jobs, and strengthens energy security by diversifying supply and decentralizing grids. Integrating renewables requires investment in infrastructure, storage solutions like batteries and pumped hydro, and smart-grid management to balance intermittent generation with demand. Policy measures, including subsidies, carbon pricing, and supportive regulations, accelerate deployment while community engagement ensures equitable access and mitigates social impacts. In many regions, combining energy efficiency with renewables yields the greatest environmental and economic benefits. Challenges remain—land use, resource variability, and initial costs—but declining technology prices and improved grid integration continue to overcome these barriers. Ultimately, renewable energy provides a practical pathway to limit climate change, foster sustainable development, and ensure reliable power for future generations, provided governments, businesses, and citizens collaborate to scale solutions responsibly. Education and international cooperation will be crucial to share best practices, finance projects in developing countries, and train workers for the low-carbon economy over the coming decades.

Explanation: The composition is correct because it succinctly covers major renewable sources, their benefits, key challenges, and the technical and policy solutions needed, giving a balanced overview. This helps students grasp that transitioning to renewables is both practical and complex, requiring coordinated technological, political, and social action.
