Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Gulshan, Dhaka-120018 January 2025Dear Tonny,How are you? Surely you are hale and hearty by the grace of almighty Allah. I am also well by his grace. However, you might be astonished to know that we have arranged a picnic at Coat Bari, Comilla. And the venue is Sonargaon. It is a historical place. You will find many kinds of old relics and can know the unknown. In fact, this place has charmed us with ancient heritage. We went there by bus. Reaching there at first we observed the relics of ancient buildings. We will also take our musical instruments with us. Our batch will take part in different games. Explanation:
The model letter is correct because it uses a warm, personal tone, clearly states the invitation, and gives key details (when to come, where to stay, and what activities to expect) so Robin can decide. A proper invitation letter follows a simple structure: greeting, brief reason for the invitation, specific dates or duration, suggested activities or arrangements, and a polite closing asking for a reply. This structure makes the message clear, courteous, and easy for the nephew to respond to.

ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক উত্তরটি তাই কারণ এতে বাসের তারিখ, সময়, রুট, যাত্রীর নাম, আসন-পছন্দ ও যোগাযোগ নম্বরসহ প্রয়োজনীয় সব তথ্য এবং ভদ্র অনুরোধ স্পষ্টভাবে দেয়া হয়েছে, ফলে ম্যানেজার সহজে টিকিট বুক করতে পারবেন। এছাড়া ই-মেইলের সাবজেক্ট, সম্ভাষণ, সংক্ষিপ্ত মূল অংশ এবং সমাপ্তি রাখলে যোগাযোগ পেশাগত ও কার্যকরি হয়।

Question:
Suppose, you want to buy a computer. Now write an e-mail to a computer agency in answer to an advertisement in the newspaper of computer that you wish to buy. Ask for details.

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: sales_cc@yahoo.com

Subject: Request for Details about Computer

Dear Sir,

I hope you are doing well. I saw your advertisement in the newspaper about a newly launched computer produced by Microsoft and distributed by your company. The computer looks quite useful for my studies and home use.

However, I would like to know the detailed specifications of the computer such as processor type, RAM, hard disk capacity, price, operating system, and warranty. I would be grateful if you could send all this information to my email.

Rabbi Rahman

81, Segun Bagicha, Dhaka

Question #59 (ID: 238020)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, your school ID card is lost. Now write an e-mail to the Headmaster of your school requesting him to issue a new one.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: headmaster@your-school.edu.bd

Subject: Request for a New School ID Card

Dear Sir,

I am a student of class 7 in your school. I would like to inform you that I have lost my school ID card on my way home yesterday. I searched everywhere but could not find it.

As it is very important for entering the school and borrowing books from the library, I kindly request you to issue me a new ID card. I am ready to follow any procedure and pay the necessary fee if required.

Thanking you,

Arif Rahman

Class 7, Roll: 24

Explanation:
সঠিক ইমেইলটি স্পষ্টভাবে সমস্যাটি জানায় — "আইডি হারিয়েছে" এবং নতুন ইস্যু করা অনুরোধ করে — পাশাপাশি প্রয়োজনীয় ব্যক্তিগত তথ্য (নাম, শ্রেণি, রোল নম্বর) দেয়, তাই হেডমাস্টার দ্রুত জানতে পারেন কাদের জন্য আবেদন। এটি বিনয়সুচক ও সংক্ষিপ্ত ভাষায় লেখা থাকে এবং বিষয় (subject) ও সম্ভাব্য দরখাস্তকারী কিস্তি/ফি বা পরিচয় প্রদানের প্রস্তুতি উল্লেখ করলে প্রক্রিয়া দ্রুত ও সঠিকভাবে সম্পন্ন হয়।

Question #60 (ID: 238021)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, you were absent in school due to illness. Now write an e-mail to your class teacher requesting him/her to excuse your absence.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: classteacher@your-school.edu.bd

Subject: Request to Excuse My Absence

Dear Sir/Madam,

I hope you are doing well. I am writing to let you know that I was unable to attend school from 2 May to 4 May because I was suffering from fever.

I have taken proper rest and treatment and now I am better. I kindly request you to excuse my absence for those days and allow me to continue my classes regularly.

<brSincerely,

Sumaiya Akter

Class 6, Roll: 15

Explanation:
This email is correct because it politely informs the teacher about your illness, states the dates you were absent, and clearly requests that your absence be excused, which shows respect and responsibility. It follows a simple structure—subject line, greeting, brief reason with dates, request for excuse, and a polite closing with your name and class—making it easy for the teacher to understand and act. Keep the language short and respectful, and attach a medical note if available to support your request.

Robin

Zila: Mymensingh

Write me back soon!

Your friend,

Robin

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: nafisa@yahoo.com

Subject: I Performed on Victory Day!

Dear Nafisa,

I hope you’re doing great. I have something exciting to tell you! This year, on Victory Day, our school arranged a cultural program and I got the chance to perform on stage. It was a drama based on the Liberation War of 1971. I played the role of a young freedom fighter.

At first, I was really nervous because this was my first time on stage in front of so many people. But once the program started, I felt confident and gave my best. Everyone clapped and cheered after the drama. Even our Headmaster praised my acting! It felt like all the rehearsals and hard work finally paid off.

Your loving friend,

Shrea

Explanation:

Question #68 (ID: 238029)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Imagine, you are Labib/Labiba. You have a friend named Richard in the USA. Now, write an e-mail to your friend inviting him to visit your country.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: labib2003@hotmail.com

Subject: Invitation to Visit Our Beautiful Bangladesh

Dear Richard,

I hope you are doing well. I was very glad to receive your last email where you showed great interest in my country, Bangladesh. As your friend, it would be an honour and joy to invite you to visit our country.

Bangladesh is a land of natural beauty. The green fields, flowing rivers, and chirping birds make this land a piece of paradise. You will fall in love with our countryside, friendly people, and delicious food. There are many tourist spots like the Shat Gambuj Mosque in Bagerhat, Mahasthangarh, the beautiful Sundarbans forest, and the long sandy beach of Cox’s Bazar. These places will give you a memorable experience of culture and nature.

So please don’t delay! Make a plan and come to visit. I promise you will have an amazing time here. Let me know your decision soon so that I can make arrangements.

Looking forward to hearing from you.

Yours lovingly,

Labib

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: আমন্ত্রণ ইমেইলটি সঠিক কারণ এতে পাঠকের উদ্দেশ্য পরিষ্কারভাবে বলা আছে — রিচার্ডকে ভ্রমণে আমন্ত্রণ দেওয়া — এবং প্রয়োজনীয় তথ্য যেমন সম্ভাব্য তারিখ, থাকার ব্যবস্থা ও যোগাযোগের মাধ্যম দেওয়া আছে। এমন ইমেইলে সৌজন্যমূলক স্বর, স্পষ্ট উদ্দেশ্য ও বাস্তব তথ্য থাকা উচিত যাতে প্রাপক সহজে পরিকল্পনা করতে পারে। তাই স্বাগত জানানোর ইচ্ছা, সময় ও সুবিধার উল্লেখ ইমেইলটিকে কার্যকর ও গ্রহণযোগ্য করে তোলে।

Question:
Suppose, you have a pen friend in the UK. He/she is very enthusiastic to know about your country, particularly her natural beauty. So, inform him/her of the natural beauty of Bangladesh through an e-mail.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: romeo_uk@yahoo.com

Subject: About the Natural Beauty of Bangladesh

Dear Romeo,

I hope you are fine. I was glad to know that you are very interested in the natural beauty of my country, Bangladesh. It’s truly a land blessed with unlimited natural charms — rivers, hills, beaches, forests, and green villages all around.

You might be amazed to know that we have the world’s longest sea beach at Cox’s Bazar. The Sundarbans, the largest mangrove forest, is home to the royal Bengal tiger. In Sylhet, you’ll see tea gardens on green hills. There are also historical places like Mahasthangarh and the Shat Gambuj Mosque. All these places attract many tourists from different parts of the world.

If you ever visit Bangladesh, I will take you to see all these places. I’m sure you’ll love the people, food, and traditions here.

<brYour friend,

Azad

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এই ইমেলটি সঠিক কারণ এটি বন্ধুসুলভ ভঙ্গিতে বাংলাদেশের প্রধান প্রাকৃতিক সৌন্দর্যগুলোর সংক্ষিপ্ত ও জীবন্ত বর্ণনা দেয় — যেমন সুন্দরবন, কক্সবাজার, চা-বাগান, নদী ও পাহাড়। এতে ব্যক্তিগত অভিজ্ঞতা ও আমন্ত্রণ যোগ করা হয়েছে, যা পাঠকের কৌতূহল বাড়ায় এবং ভিজ্যুয়াল ধারণা দেয়। সংক্ষিপ্ততা, স্নেহপূর্ণ ভাষা ও নির্দিষ্ট উদাহরণ থাকার ফলে এটি একটি উপযুক্ত Pen-friend ইমেল মডেল।

Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Inform your mother through e-mail how you physically feel after recovery from an ailment.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: samad@hotmail.com

Subject: About My Recovery and Health Condition

My sweet Mum,

I hope you are doing well. I received your email asking about my health and I want to let you know that I am now completely fine. The fever is gone and I feel much better now.

The doctor advised me to eat healthy food and take enough rest. I have also started light exercises as suggested. I am trying to maintain a proper routine now. Please don’t worry about me anymore. I will be more careful from now on and take good care of my health.

<brPlease share this happy news with Dad and everyone at home. Miss you so much.

Your loving son,

Joy

Explanation:
The correct answer works because it clearly and honestly tells your mother which symptoms have improved and how your daily energy and activities are now, so she can understand your current health. When reporting recovery, focus on specific changes (e.g., fever gone, appetite returned, more energy), note any remaining weakness or medication/rest needs, and give a brief reassurance. Use simple, calm language so the message is easy to read and helps your mother know whether further care is needed.

Question #77 (ID: 238038)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, your friend has recently been sick. Write an e-mail to your friend wishing him/her a speedy recovery.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
To: nabila.care@gmail.com

Subject: Wishing You a Quick Recovery

Dear Nabila,

I was really sorry to hear that you have been unwell for the past few days. I hope you are taking proper rest and following the doctor’s advice. I know it’s hard to stay away from school and friends, but your health is the most important right now.

We all miss you in class. Even our class teacher asked about you. The classroom feels incomplete without your cheerful presence. Don’t worry about the lessons — I’ve been taking notes for you and will help you catch up once you return. Just focus on your recovery now.

May Allah bless you with good health very soon. We’re all waiting to see you back at school, smiling like before.

Get well soon!

Your friend,

Fahim

Explanation:
A get-well email is appropriate because it shows care and offers emotional support without demanding much energy from your sick friend. Include a brief expression of concern, a sincere wish for a speedy recovery, an offer to help (e.g., run errands or bring medicine), and a warm closing to keep the tone caring and respectful. Short, specific, and sincere messages are most comforting and practical when someone is unwell.

এই আবেদনপত্রটি সঠিক কারণ এতে আবেদনকারীর নাম ও শ্রেণি, স্টাডি ট্যুরের উদ্দেশ্য এবং প্রধানবিদ্যালয়ের কাছে বিনীতভাবে অনুমতি চাওয়ার অনুরোধ স্পষ্টভাবে উল্লেখ আছে। ভদ্র ভাষা, সঠিক তারিখ ও যোগাযোগের তথ্য দিলে প্রধানের পক্ষে আবেদনটি দ্রুত মূল্যায়ন ও অনুমোদন করা সহজ হয়। তাই আবেদনটি সংক্ষিপ্ত ও গঠনগতভাবে সঠিক হওয়াই মূল কৌশল।

Subject: Prayer for arranging a cultural function.

Dear Sir,

We, the students of class VI, would like to organize a cultural function in our school auditorium. We want to perform songs, poems, and drama to express our talent and boost our confidence.

We request you to kindly grant us permission and allow us the necessary support including sound system and seating arrangements. We hope you will encourage us.

Yours obediently,

Sabbir

Class VI, Roll No. 09

Explanation:
এই আবেদনটি সঠিক কারণ এতে প্রধান শিক্ষকের প্রতি নম্রভাবে সম্বোধন আছে, অনুষ্ঠানের উদ্দেশ্য ও তার তারিখ‑সময় পরিষ্কারভাবে উল্লেখ করা হয়েছে এবং অনুমতি ও প্রয়োজনীয় সহায়তা চাওয়া হয়েছে। ফর্মাল আবেদন লেখার মূল ধারণা হলো সুস্পষ্ট অনুরোধ করা, প্রয়োজনীয় তথ্য (ক্লাস, ছাত্র সংখ্য, প্রয়োজনীয় জিনিসপত্র) দেওয়া এবং ভদ্র ভাষা রাখা যাতে কর্তৃপক্ষ দ্রুত সিদ্ধান্ত নিতে পারেন। তাই আবেদনপত্রে সংক্ষিপ্ত ও নির্ভুল তথ্য এবং আবেদনকারীর সই/ক্লাসের উল্লেখ থাকা প্রয়োজন।

Question #92 (ID: 238053)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{A Journey by Boat}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{A Journey by Boat}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is a land of rivers, so boat journeys are very common here. A journey by boat is a wonderful way to enjoy nature and relax from the busy life of towns or cities. I had such a journey last year, and it became one of my most memorable experiences.[math]\textbf{Planning and Preparation:}[/math]
 It was during my autumn vacation. I planned a trip with two close friends from Kotwalipara to Gopalganj. We hired a country boat and two boatmen. We also packed some dry food, water bottles, clothes, and a camera to take pictures.[math]\textbf{Starting the Journey:}[/math]
 The weather was perfect that morning. The river was calm and the sky was clear. As the boatmen hoisted the sail, the boat slowly moved forward. A gentle breeze added comfort to our journey. We sat comfortably and enjoyed the surroundings.[math]\textbf{Beauty and Enjoyment:}[/math]
 On both sides of the river, we saw green paddy fields, jute plants, and trees full of flowers. Children were playing near the riverbanks. We heard birds chirping and saw fishermen casting their nets. Everything looked like a painting of peace and joy.[math]\textbf{End of the Journey:}[/math]
 After four hours, we reached Gopalganj safely. We were tired but extremely happy.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 This boat journey gave me a deep connection with nature. It was peaceful, joyful, and refreshing. I wish to enjoy such a journey again.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: একটি সফল 'A Journey by Boat' রচনা সঠিক কারণ এতে স্পষ্ট সূচনা, ক্রমানুসারে ঘটনার বর্ণনা এবং সমাপ্তিতে লেখকের অনুভূতি বা শিক্ষা আছে; পরিবেশ描写 (নদী/সাগর, নৌকার শব্দ ও গতি) এবং সংক্ষিপ্ত ঘটনাবলি রচনাটিকে জীবনমান দেয়। ভাল রচনায় বর্ণনামূলক শব্দচয়ন, সহজ বাক্যগঠন ও বিষয়ের সংহততা বজায় রেখে ২০০ শব্দের মধ্যে দৃশ্য, পাঠকসংযোগ ও উপসংহার স্পষ্ট রাখাটাই মৌলিক ধারণা।

Question #93 (ID: 238054)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Importance of Reading Newspaper}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Importance of Reading Newspaper}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Newspapers are a window to the world. They inform us about current events, government decisions, social issues, and more. In modern life, reading newspapers has become a daily habit and a part of our routine.[math]\textbf{Types of Newspapers:}[/math]
 There are dailies, weeklies, and monthlies. Dailies provide everyday news, while weeklies and monthlies give us in-depth reports, opinions, and feature articles. Newspapers can be in printed form or digital format nowadays.[math]\textbf{Educational Importance:}[/math]
 For students, newspapers are very useful. They help us improve our vocabulary, knowledge, and general awareness. Many schools encourage students to read newspapers daily to stay updated.[math]\textbf{Social and National Role:}[/math]
 Newspapers help people understand social, political, and economic issues. They inform citizens about elections, government policies, and national events. They also help create public opinion and spread awareness.[math]\textbf{Entertainment and Career:}[/math]
 Apart from news, newspapers also provide entertainment through cartoons, puzzles, horoscopes, and comics. They also publish job circulars, exam results, and advertisements that help in career planning.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Reading newspapers regularly is a good habit. It increases our knowledge and keeps us aware of the world around us. In the age of digital media, newspapers still hold great value as a trusted source of information.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: একটি ভালো ২০০-শব্দের রচনা সংবাদপত্র পড়ার কারণগুলো সংক্ষিপ্ত ও শ্রেণীবদ্ধভাবে তুলে ধরে — যেমন বর্তমান ঘটনার জ্ঞান, ভাষা ও শব্দভাণ্ডারের উন্নতি, এবং সমালোচনামূলক চিন্তার বিকাশ। রচনায় প্রাসঙ্গিক উদাহরণ ও ফলাফল দেখালে পাঠকের কাছে বক্তব্যটিকে বিশ্বাসযোগ্য এবং প্রয়োজনীয়ভাবে স্থাপন করা যায়। তাই এসব উপাদান থাকার কারণে রচনাটি সঠিক, পরিষ্কার এবং শিক্ষণীয় বলে বিবেচিত হয়।

Question #94 (ID: 238055)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{My Future Plan of Life}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{My Future Plan of Life}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Every person should have a plan for the future. Without a clear goal, life becomes uncertain and confusing. I have made a decision about what I want to become in life and how I wish to serve others.[math]\textbf{My Aim:}[/math]
 I want to become a doctor. From a young age, I have seen people around me suffer due to lack of proper medical care. I want to treat the poor and bring relief to the sick. This aim inspires me to work hard.[math]\textbf{Reason Behind My Choice:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is a developing country. Many villages do not have hospitals or trained doctors. The poor people cannot afford costly treatment. I want to serve them by giving free medical care and advice.[math]\textbf{My Preparation:}[/math]
 I am a student of class 10 now. I study science subjects seriously. After SSC, I want to get admitted to a good medical college. I will then work in rural areas to serve those in need.[math]\textbf{My Intention:}[/math]
 I also want to open a small clinic in my village. I will treat the people with love and care. This will be my way of giving back to society.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Life is valuable when it is spent for others. My dream is to become a doctor and help my country. I believe this is a noble and meaningful goal.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ভালো "My Future Plan of Life" রচনা সঠিক কারণ এতে পরিচিতি, প্রধান লক্ষ্য, অর্জনের জন্য নেওয়া পদক্ষেপ ও উপসংহার পরিষ্কার ও সুবিন্যস্তভাবে উপস্থাপিত থাকে এবং নির্ধারিত ২০০ শব্দের মধ্যে বিষয়টি সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করা হয়। এটি পাঠককে লেখকের ভবিষ্যৎ লক্ষ্য, সেই লক্ষ্য কেন গুরুত্বপূর্ণ এবং তা অর্জনে প্রয়োজনীয় শিক্ষা ও দক্ষতা অর্জনের বাস্তবধর্মী ধাপগুলো স্পষ্টভাবে জানায়। মূল ধারণা হল—সুসংগঠিত কাঠামো, বাস্তবসম্মত লক্ষ্য এবং স্পষ্ট কর্মপরিকল্পনা রাখা; এসব থাকার কারণে রচনাটি যুক্তিযুক্ত ও শিক্ষণীয়।

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Tree Plantation}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Tree Plantation}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Trees are an important part of our environment. They give us life and support the balance of nature. Without trees, we cannot survive. So tree plantation is not only necessary, it is a duty for all of us.[math]\textbf{Benefits of Trees:}[/math]
 Trees provide oxygen, shade, and fruits. They absorb carbon dioxide and reduce air pollution. They stop soil erosion, bring rain, and keep the weather pleasant. Trees are home to many birds and animals.[math]\textbf{Economic and Health Benefits:}[/math]
 Trees give us wood, medicine, and raw materials. They reduce stress, make our surroundings peaceful, and help us live longer. Parks and gardens with trees make cities more livable.[math]\textbf{Condition in Bangladesh:}[/math]
 Our country needs more trees. According to experts, 25% of land should be forested, but we have much less. Deforestation is harming our environment.[math]\textbf{Best Time and Awareness:}[/math]
 The rainy season is the best time for planting trees. Schools, colleges, and government offices should organize tree plantation programs. People should be aware of its importance and join such efforts.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Tree plantation is a great act of service to nature and future generations. If every person plants and cares for at least one tree, we can make our world greener and better.

Explanation:
এই রচনাটি সঠিক কারণ এতে গাছ রোপণের গুরুত্ব, পরিবেশগত উপকারিতা এবং রোপণের পদ্ধতি পরপরভাবে উপস্থাপিত আছে — প্রস্তাবনা, মূল অংশ এবং উপসংহার স্পষ্ট। এটি বোঝায় যে গাছ শুদ্ধ বায়ু, ছায়া, মাটির সংরক্ষণ ও জীববৈচিত্র্য দেয় এবং ব্যক্তিগত ও সামাজিকভাবে গাছ লাগানো ও পরিচর্যা করা জরুরি। রচনা লেখার সময় সরল ভাষা, বাস্তব উদাহরণ ও কার্যকর সমাপ্তি দিলে পাঠক কেন গাছ লাগানো উচিত এবং কীভাবে করতে হবে তা সহজে বুঝতে পারে।

Question #96 (ID: 238057)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Physical Exercise}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Physical Exercise}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Physical exercise means the regular movement of body parts. It is essential for good health. Just as food is necessary for our body, exercise is also needed to keep us active and strong.[math]\textbf{Types of Exercise:}[/math]
 There are many kinds of physical exercise — walking, running, swimming, cycling, skipping, and yoga. Games like football, cricket, and badminton are also good forms of exercise. People of all ages should choose exercises according to their strength and age.[math]\textbf{Importance of Exercise:}[/math]
 Physical exercise keeps our body fit, increases blood circulation, and improves our immune system. It makes us energetic and helps us concentrate better in studies. A person who exercises regularly remains fresh and cheerful.[math]\textbf{Best Time and Place:}[/math]
 Early morning is the best time for exercise because the air is clean and cool. Open spaces like parks, gardens, and fields are suitable places. Fresh air adds to the benefits.[math]\textbf{Mental and Social Value:}[/math]
 Exercise also improves our mood and reduces stress. It helps us socialize, build friendships, and learn discipline through sports.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 A healthy mind lives in a healthy body. Without exercise, we cannot enjoy life fully. So, everyone should do some form of physical activity daily to stay fit and happy.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it defines [math]\textbf{Physical Exercise}[/math], describes its main types (aerobic, strength, flexibility), and gives clear examples and benefits such as improved heart health, stronger muscles, weight control, and better mental well‑being. It helps students grasp the underlying concept by linking everyday activities to physiological effects—better circulation, increased metabolism, and reduced stress—so they see how and why exercise improves health. The language and structure are simple and focused, enabling students to reproduce a balanced 200‑word essay that covers purpose, benefits, types, and safe ways to practice exercise.

Question #97 (ID: 238058)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Duties of a Student}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Duties of a Student}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 A student’s life is the most important part of a person's life. It is called the golden period because this is the time for learning and building character. A student has many responsibilities not only to himself but also to society and the country.[math]\textbf{Duties to Education:}[/math]
 The first and foremost duty of a student is to study with full attention. He must attend school regularly, listen to teachers, complete homework, and prepare for exams sincerely. Good education is the foundation of a successful life.[math]\textbf{Duties to Parents and Teachers:}[/math]
 A student must respect parents and teachers. Parents provide love and support, while teachers guide and shape our future. Obeying and honoring them is a sacred duty.[math]\textbf{Duties to Society:}[/math]
 Students should be aware of the needs of society. They can help in literacy programs, cleanliness drives, and disaster relief. They should avoid bad habits and try to become honest and active citizens.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 A student must grow up with discipline, honesty, and a strong sense of duty. By performing their duties properly, students can build a better future for themselves and for the country.

Explanation:
এই রচনা সঠিক কারণ এতে শিক্ষার্থীর প্রধান কর্তব্য—পরিশ্রমী পড়াশোনা, শৃঙ্খলা ও সময়নিষ্ঠা, সততা, শিক্ষক ও অভিভাবকের প্রতি শ্রদ্ধা, সামাজিক ও পরিবেশগত দায়িত্ব—সংক্ষেপে ও সুসংগঠিতভাবে উপস্থাপন করা হয়েছে এবং পরিচিতি, প্রধান অংশ ও উপসংহার রেখে ২০০ শব্দের মধ্যে প্রয়োজনীয় বিষয়গুলি কভার করা হয়েছে। মূল ধারণা হলো শিক্ষার্থীর কর্তব্য ব্যক্তি ও সমাজের উন্নয়ন নিশ্চিত করে, কিন্তু সেটি বোঝাতে বাস্তব উদাহরণ ও নৈতিক ব্যাখ্যা যোগ করা জরুরি। সুতরাং স্পষ্ট ধারাবাহিকতা, সহজ ভাষা ও সংক্ষিপ্ত উপসংহার দিয়ে রচনা করলে এটি সঠিক ও কার্যকর হবে।

Nature seems to wear a new dress in spring, and everything looks colorful and pleasant.[math]\textbf{Comparison with Other Seasons:}[/math]
 Compared to summer, which is very hot and sometimes unbearable, spring is very enjoyable. Unlike the rainy season that often brings floods and suffering, spring brings joy and happiness. Winter is too cold for many people, but spring has a balanced temperature. Neither too hot nor too cold — it is just perfect. That is why spring stands out among all the seasons.[math]\textbf{Beauty of Spring:}[/math]
 Spring is the season of flowers and greenery. Trees get new leaves, and flowers bloom everywhere. Birds sing sweet songs. Bees fly from flower to flower. Explanation:

Keep simple language, logical order, and smooth transitions so the reader easily follows your reasons and the piece fits the required length.

Question #105 (ID: 238066)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Value of Time}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Value of Time}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Time is the most valuable thing in our life. It is more precious than money, gold, or anything else. Once time is gone, it never returns. So, we must value every second and use time wisely.[math]\textbf{Importance in Life:}[/math]
 Everything in the world follows time. The sun rises and sets on time. Trains and planes run according to schedule. If we do not use time properly, we fall behind in life. Time helps us become successful and respected.[math]\textbf{Time for Students:}[/math]
 Student life is the best time to build a future. Those who study regularly, follow routine, and do everything on time become good students. Laziness and delay bring failure and sadness. So, students should make good use of their time.[math]\textbf{Famous Quotes:}[/math]
 There is a saying — “Time and tide wait for none.” This teaches us that we must not waste time. Another saying is — “Work while you work, play while you play.” This tells us that everything has a proper time.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Time is like a sword — if we do not cut with it, it will cut us. Success and happiness depend on proper use of time. So, we should always be punctual, organized, and never waste time.

Explanation:
The value of time is one of the most important lessons in life. Time is a non-renewable resource; once spent it cannot be regained, so using it wisely determines success, happiness, and growth. Punctuality, planning, and prioritizing tasks help individuals make the most of every hour. Procrastination, on the other hand, wastes opportunities and increases stress. Respecting other people's time builds trust and shows professionalism. Time management techniques like setting clear goals, breaking tasks into smaller steps, and using schedules or timers increase efficiency and reduce distractions. Investing time in learning, health, and relationships yields long-term benefits that compound, much like financial investments. Young people should develop habits early—consistent study routines, disciplined work ethics, and regular reflection—so they can achieve long-term aims. In daily life small choices matter: arriving five minutes early, preparing the night before, or limiting social media can free up hours each week. Balancing work and rest is also crucial; adequate rest ensures sustained productivity and avoids burnout. Ultimately, valuing time means recognizing its scarcity, prioritizing what truly matters, and acting deliberately. When we treat time as precious, we make better decisions and create a life that reflects our deepest goals. Value time; it shapes your future.

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Graffiti: Art as Protest in the July Revolution}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Graffiti: Art as Protest in the July Revolution}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Graffiti is a form of street art made on public surfaces like walls, buildings, or roads. It is not just art for beauty but often used as a powerful medium to express strong emotions, political opinions, and social messages. It can represent unity, resistance, and the voice of the voiceless.[math]\textbf{Graffiti in the July Revolution:}[/math]
 During the July Revolution of 2024 in Bangladesh, graffiti became a key symbol of protest. Students and activists used graffiti to raise voices against injustice. One famous mural was painted with the question, “Who will bring justice for the murder of martyr Abu Sayeed?” Even though it was removed the next day, the message left a deep impact on society.[math]\textbf{After the Fall of the Government:}[/math]
 On August 5, 2024, after the fall of the dictatorial regime, graffiti spread across cities and towns. Walls in Dhaka were filled with slogans like “Lakho shaheeder rokte kena, deshta karo baper na!” — a protest against selling the sacrifices of martyrs. Symbols like clenched fists and rising suns were drawn to inspire strength and revolution.[math]\textbf{Unity and Artistic Protest:}[/math]
 Graffiti united students, artists, rickshaw pullers, and common people. It gave them a voice. Donations were raised through graffiti campaigns. It became more than art — it became a tool of unity, awareness, and hope.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Graffiti played a vital role during the July Revolution. It empowered the people, carried their pain and anger, and turned walls into voices. It will be remembered as a unique form of protest that changed minds and gave people courage.

Explanation:
Writing a composition on "Graffiti: Art as Protest in the July Revolution" is appropriate because graffiti functioned as an immediate, public form of political speech that captured protesters’ demands, symbols, and emotions on city walls. The underlying concept is that graffiti transforms ordinary urban space into a visual forum for dissent—its accessibility, bold imagery, and short, memorable messages make it an effective tool for mobilization, solidarity, and historical memory. In your 200‑word piece, emphasize the historical context, notable motifs or slogans, how graffiti communicated ideas to broad audiences, and its lasting role in shaping collective memory and protest identities.

Question #107 (ID: 238068)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Anti-discrimination Student Movement}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Anti-discrimination Student Movement}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 The Anti-discrimination Student Movement was one of the biggest student-led protests in Bangladesh in recent times. It happened in July 2024 and started because students were unhappy about the unfair job quota system announced by the government.[math]\textbf{The Cause of Protest:}[/math]
 In June 2024, the High Court of Bangladesh declared a 30% quota for children of freedom fighters in government jobs. However, there were already quotas for other groups. As a result, only 44% of jobs remained open for general applicants. Students believed this system was unjust and demanded a fair distribution of opportunities.[math]\textbf{Historical Background:}[/math]
 This protest was not new. Students had previously protested against quota systems in 2013 and 2018. Those movements created awareness, but in 2024, the issue became more serious and widespread.[math]\textbf{Nature of the Protest:}[/math]
 Students across the country took to the streets. They blocked major roads and organized sit-ins. On July 15, the protest turned violent when armed individuals attacked students. Many were injured. Yet, the protests grew stronger. Social media helped spread the movement quickly.[math]\textbf{Demand and Result:}[/math]
 On August 3, students declared that the government must resign. Their demand was bold, but it showed their frustration. They wanted fairness, not privilege based on birth. The protest was about equality, merit, and justice.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 The Anti-discrimination Student Movement was a powerful example of student unity and courage. It reminded the nation that youth will rise against injustice. The movement has made a permanent mark on Bangladesh’s political and social history.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক উত্তরটি কারণসূচকভাবে আন্দোলনের সংজ্ঞা, বৈষম্যের কারণ, শিক্ষার্থীদের নেওয়া কর্মসূচি এবং তাদের অর্জিত সাফল্য/গুরত্ব সংক্ষেপে উপস্থাপন করে; এতে পাঠক সহজেই বিষয়টি ধরতে পারে। এটি ধারণাগতভাবে বোঝায় যে বিরোধিতা শুধু অবিচারের বিরুদ্ধে নয়, বরং সমতা, মানবাধিকার এবং শিক্ষাগত অন্তর্ভুক্তির জন্য সংগঠিত সংগ্রাম, এবং এতে ছাত্রসংগঠন, প্রতিবাদ, সচেতনতা ও নীতি পরিবর্তনের ভূমিকা স্পষ্ট করা হয়। সংগঠিত ও ধারাবাহিক বিন্যাস (ভূমিকা, বিষয়বস্তু, উপসংহার) এবং নির্দিষ্ট উদাহরণগুলো নিয়ে ২০০ শব্দের মধ্যে থাকা উত্তরটি পাঠ্য ও কার্যকারিতা উভয় দিক থেকে সঠিক।

Question #108 (ID: 238069)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Artificial Intelligence}[/math] in 200 words.

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Artificial Intelligence}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Artificial Intelligence (AI) is one of the most revolutionary technologies of the 21st century. It refers to the ability of machines to mimic human intelligence and behavior. AI enables machines to learn from experience, adjust to new inputs, and perform tasks that normally require human thinking. From smart assistants on our phones to robots performing surgery, AI is rapidly transforming our world.[math]\textbf{Applications:}[/math]
 AI is used in a wide range of fields. In healthcare, it helps in early diagnosis, robotic surgery, and patient monitoring. In education, AI can personalize learning for students. In business, AI helps in data analysis, customer support, and fraud detection. Self-driving cars, language translation tools, and facial recognition systems are some daily uses of AI. Even in agriculture, AI is used to predict weather, manage irrigation, and monitor crops using drones.[math]\textbf{Advantages:}[/math]
 AI offers many benefits. It increases efficiency, reduces human effort, and performs repetitive tasks faster. AI systems can operate 24/7 and handle large volumes of data quickly. It helps industries grow faster and makes our lives more convenient. In dangerous jobs like mining, firefighting, or space exploration, AI-based robots are lifesavers.[math]\textbf{Challenges and Concerns:}[/math]
 Despite its advantages, AI has some drawbacks. It may cause unemployment as machines replace human workers. There are ethical concerns like data privacy, bias in algorithms, and misuse in warfare or surveillance. If misused, AI can be harmful. Over-dependence on machines may reduce human thinking abilities.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Artificial Intelligence is not just a trend — it is the future. It has the potential to solve global problems and improve life in countless ways. But we must ensure its responsible and ethical use. Governments, tech companies, and citizens must work together to build an AI-powered world that benefits all of humanity.

Explanation:
A good 200-word composition on Artificial Intelligence is correct when it succinctly defines AI, gives a few clear examples of applications (like healthcare, automation, and assistants), and mentions its benefits and key challenges such as bias, privacy, and job impact. This works because AI fundamentally means machines performing tasks that require human-like learning, reasoning, or perception, so showing concrete examples and implications demonstrates understanding. The 200-word limit requires focused structure—brief definition, illustrative applications, and a sentence on ethical or societal concerns—to cover the essential concept clearly and concisely.

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{My Country (Bangladesh)}[/math] in 200 words.

Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{My Country (Bangladesh)}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is my beloved motherland. It is a beautiful and peaceful country in South Asia. Despite being a small country in size, it is rich in culture, history, and natural beauty. The country became independent in 1971 after a nine-month-long liberation war against Pakistan. The people of Bangladesh are brave, hardworking, and kind-hearted.[math]\textbf{Geography and Nature:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is a land of rivers. More than 700 rivers flow through the country, including the Padma, Jamuna, and Meghna. The land is flat and fertile, which supports agriculture. It has green fields, forests, hills, and the world-famous Sundarbans, the largest mangrove forest. Cox’s Bazar, the longest sea beach in the world, attracts tourists from around the globe.[math]\textbf{People and Culture:}[/math]
 The people of Bangladesh are mostly Bengali and speak Bangla, the national language. The culture is rich with folk songs, dance, literature, and festivals. Pahela Baishakh (Bengali New Year), Eid-ul-Fitr, and Durga Puja are widely celebrated. People wear traditional clothes and share joy with friends and families.[math]\textbf{Economy and Development:}[/math]
 The economy of Bangladesh is developing fast. It depends on agriculture, garments, remittances, and the IT sector. Many people work in the garment industry, which earns foreign currency. Bangladesh is making progress in education, health, and technology under the vision of “Digital Bangladesh.”[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Although Bangladesh faces challenges like poverty, traffic, and natural disasters, the people are hopeful and strong. I am proud to be a citizen of this land. I dream of contributing to its progress and showing the world how beautiful and brave Bangladesh is.

Explanation:
This composition is correct because it gives a clear introduction about Bangladesh, describes its geography, history, culture, economy and achievements, and ends with a concluding sentence expressing pride—covering the essential points expected in a 200-word essay. It follows a logical structure (topic sentence, supporting details, conclusion), uses simple coherent sentences and linking words, and includes specific facts or examples to make ideas concrete. By staying within the word limit and using clear vocabulary and varied sentence structure, it meets the assignment requirements and helps the reader understand and appreciate the country.

Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Birds of Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Birds of Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Bangladesh, being a country of forests, rivers, and wetlands, is home to a wide variety of birds. The natural environment of the country supports both resident and migratory birds. Birds not only add beauty to nature but also play a vital role in maintaining ecological balance.[math]\textbf{Common Birds:}[/math]
 Some common birds in Bangladesh include the crow, sparrow, myna, dove, woodpecker, and parrot. The cuckoo is famous for its sweet song, especially in spring. The kingfisher is often seen near rivers, diving for fish. The kite and eagle are birds of prey. In rural areas, the presence of hen, duck, and pigeon is also very common.[math]\textbf{Migratory Birds:}[/math]
 During winter, thousands of migratory birds come from Siberia and other colder regions. They gather around lakes, wetlands, and haors in places like Hakaluki Haor and Tanguar Haor. Their arrival creates a festive atmosphere for bird watchers and nature lovers.[math]\textbf{Importance of Birds:}[/math]
 Birds are essential for nature. They help in pollination, seed spreading, and controlling pests. Their nests on trees make forests lively. The songs of birds bring peace and joy to people’s minds. They are also part of folklore and folk songs in Bengali culture.[math]\textbf{Threats and Protection:}[/math]
 Birds in Bangladesh face many threats, such as deforestation, hunting, and habitat destruction. Illegal bird trade and pollution are also harming them. Public awareness, bird sanctuaries, and wildlife laws are needed to protect them.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Birds are valuable to our country’s nature and culture. We must protect them for future generations. Everyone should learn to love and preserve birds and their habitats.

Explanation:

Question #111 (ID: 238072)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{The Rivers of Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{The Rivers of Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is often referred to as the “Land of Rivers.” There are more than 700 rivers crisscrossing the country. These rivers are not only a gift of nature but also the foundation of the country's agriculture, transportation, trade, and culture.[math]\textbf{Major Rivers:}[/math]
 Some of the major rivers are the Padma, Jamuna, Meghna, Brahmaputra, Teesta, Surma, and Karnaphuli. These rivers help in irrigation, fishing, and connecting remote villages to towns and cities. Rivers are also sacred in religion and celebrated in poems and songs.[math]\textbf{Importance:}[/math]
 Rivers bring fertility to the land by depositing alluvial soil. They are vital for rice and jute farming, which are key agricultural products. People travel by boat through rivers. Fishermen catch hilsa and other fish, earning their livelihood. River ports like Narayanganj and Barisal play a role in national trade.[math]\textbf{Cultural Significance:}[/math]
 Rivers are deeply rooted in Bengali literature and art. Famous poets like Rabindranath Tagore and Jasimuddin wrote beautiful verses inspired by river life. Boat races, festivals, and folk music often happen by the riverside.[math]\textbf{Threats and Protection:}[/math]
 Unfortunately, many rivers are dying due to pollution, illegal grabbing, and overuse. Factories release toxic waste into rivers. Climate change is also affecting water flow. River protection laws and awareness campaigns are urgently needed.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Rivers are like the blood vessels of Bangladesh. To save our country, we must save our rivers. Proper care and use of rivers will ensure our future prosperity.

Explanation:
Rivers are the lifeblood of Bangladesh, shaping its landscape, culture, and economy. The country is crisscrossed by a dense network of rivers, the main ones being the Padma, Jamuna, and Meghna, which together form the vast Bengal delta. These rivers bring fertile silt that enriches the soil, supporting intensive rice cultivation and other agriculture that feed millions. They serve as vital waterways for transport and trade, connecting inland communities and reducing dependence on road infrastructure. Rivers also sustain fisheries and wetlands that support biodiversity and provide livelihoods for many rural families. Seasonal monsoon flows cause annual floods that replenish soils but also bring destruction through erosion, displacement, and damage to homes and crops. Human activities—such as deforestation, unplanned riverbank settlements, sand mining, and industrial pollution—have worsened riverbank erosion and water quality. Climate change and upstream water management further affect river regimes, increasing uncertainty for farmers and planners. Sustainable river management, integrated flood control, river dredging where appropriate, pollution control, and transboundary cooperation with upstream countries are essential to preserve these waterways. Protecting and wisely managing Bangladesh’s rivers ensures food security, economic resilience, and environmental health for future generations.

[math]\textbf{The Fruits of Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is a fertile land where a wide variety of fruits grow naturally due to its tropical climate and rich soil. Fruits are available here throughout the year in different seasons. These fruits not only add color and flavor to our meals but are also essential for our health.[math]\textbf{Seasonal Fruits:}[/math]
 Different fruits grow in different seasons. During summer, mango, jackfruit, litchi, watermelon, and pineapple are widely available. Mango is known as the king of fruits. It is juicy, sweet, and full of vitamins. Jackfruit, the national fruit of Bangladesh, is large and rich in energy. Watermelon is perfect for summer because of its high water content.[math]\textbf{Winter and All-Season Fruits:}[/math]
 In winter, oranges, guavas, custard apples, and apples are found in abundance. These fruits are rich in vitamin C and good for digestion. Bananas, coconuts, and papayas are available almost throughout the year. Papaya helps in digestion and is often prescribed by doctors.[math]\textbf{Nutritional Value:}[/math]
 Fruits are full of nutrients such as vitamins, minerals, and fiber. They boost our immune system, improve skin health, and reduce the risk of diseases. They are especially important for children and the elderly. Eating fresh fruits daily is a healthy habit.[math]\textbf{Economic Importance:}[/math]
 Many farmers in Bangladesh grow fruits commercially. Fruit farming creates employment, helps in poverty reduction, and earns foreign currency through export. Guava from Barisal and mangoes from Rajshahi are famous across the country.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Fruits are a blessing from nature. They are delicious, refreshing, and nutritious. We should eat fruits daily and encourage fruit farming. Protecting fruit trees and supporting farmers will help us build a healthier and greener Bangladesh.

Explanation:
The composition is correct because it briefly describes the main fruits of Bangladesh (e.g., mango, jackfruit, litchi, banana, coconut), their seasons and tastes, and highlights their nutritional, cultural, and economic importance. It clarifies the underlying concept by organizing information into a short introduction, focused descriptions with examples, and a concluding statement, which helps readers grasp both facts and sensory impressions. For a 200-word essay, use simple sentences, specific examples, and a logical flow so the reader learns what the fruits are, why they matter, and how they relate to Bangladeshi life.

Question #113 (ID: 238074)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Floods in Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Floods in Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is one of the most flood-prone countries in the world. Its geographical position, numerous rivers, and monsoon climate make it vulnerable to frequent floods. Although floods are natural, their impact on people and the economy can be devastating.[math]\textbf{Causes of Flood:}[/math]
 Heavy rainfall during the monsoon is the main cause of floods. Overflowing of rivers like Padma, Jamuna, and Brahmaputra submerges vast areas. Melting of Himalayan glaciers increases river water levels. Poor drainage in urban areas and deforestation make floods worse.[math]\textbf{Effects of Floods:}[/math]
 Floods damage crops, houses, roads, schools, and hospitals. Many people become homeless and have to take shelter in flood centers. Food and drinking water become scarce. Diseases like diarrhea, cholera, and skin infections spread easily. Educational activities are interrupted for weeks.[math]\textbf{Impact on Economy and Society:}[/math]
 Farmers suffer the most because their crops are washed away. Transportation stops, and business activities decline. Relief work becomes expensive and often delays. The country’s GDP is affected by repeated flood losses.[math]\textbf{Relief and Response:}[/math]
 The government and NGOs try to provide relief by supplying food, clean water, medicine, and shelter. Volunteers and local people also help flood victims. Boats and helicopters are used for rescue. Early warning systems are improving, but much more needs to be done.[math]\textbf{Prevention and }[/math]
 Building embankments, dredging rivers, planting trees, and improving drainage can reduce flood damage. Public awareness and community training are essential. Scientific forecasting systems must be upgraded.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 We cannot stop floods, but we can reduce their damage. Proper planning, strong infrastructure, and public cooperation can make Bangladesh more flood-resilient.

Explanation:
Bangladesh is one of the most flood-prone countries in the world. Each year, heavy monsoon rains, melting Himalayan snow, and overflowing rivers — especially the Ganges, Brahmaputra and Meghna systems — bring widespread inundation. Low-lying topography, high population density in floodplains, riverbank erosion and siltation make the country particularly vulnerable, while climate change is increasing the intensity and unpredictability of extreme rainfall and cyclones.

The impacts of floods are severe: loss of lives, damage to homes and infrastructure, crop failure, and outbreaks of waterborne diseases. Flooding also disrupts education and livelihoods, pushing many people into poverty and forcing seasonal or permanent migration. Short-term responses include early warning systems, community shelters, emergency relief, and distribution of food and medicine. Structural measures such as embankments, raised roads and flood shelters help reduce immediate harm, but can have environmental trade-offs if poorly planned.

Long-term solutions require integrated river basin management, improved drainage, reforestation, climate-resilient agriculture, and planned urban development that avoids high-risk zones. Strengthening local capacity, investing in adaptive infrastructure, and international cooperation on upstream water management are essential to reduce flood risks and build resilience for Bangladesh’s vulnerable communities.

Question #114 (ID: 238075)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Write a composition on [math]\textbf{Population Problem in Bangladesh}[/math] in 200 words.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]\textbf{Population Problem in Bangladesh}[/math]
 [math]\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]
 Bangladesh is one of the most densely populated countries in the world. With over 170 million people living in a small area, the country is facing serious population-related challenges. This problem affects almost every aspect of life — from food and housing to education and employment.[math]\textbf{Reasons for Overpopulation:}[/math]
 Lack of awareness about family planning, early marriage, poverty, and low literacy rates are the main reasons for overpopulation. In rural areas, people often think more children mean more help in work. Many families are unaware of the economic and social burden caused by large families.[math]\textbf{Effects of Overpopulation:}[/math]
 Overpopulation creates a huge strain on food, water, land, education, and healthcare. Schools become overcrowded, and hospitals cannot treat all patients properly. Unemployment rises, and crime rates increase. Urban areas suffer from traffic jams, pollution, and housing crises.[math]\textbf{Impact on Development:}[/math]
 Rapid population growth makes it difficult to provide quality education and job opportunities. It slows down economic progress. Resources that could be used for development are instead spent on basic needs like food and shelter. Government services become insufficient.[math]\textbf{Solutions:}[/math]
 The only way to solve this problem is through strong family planning programs, public awareness campaigns, and compulsory education for girls. Delaying marriage and promoting one or two-child families can help control growth. Religious leaders, teachers, and media can also spread awareness.[math]\textbf{Government Role:}[/math]
 The government should ensure availability of free birth control services, provide incentives for small families, and punish false registration or misuse of welfare schemes.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Population is both a strength and a challenge. If managed well, it can become a national asset. But if it continues to grow unchecked, it can destroy progress. We must act now to save our future.

Explanation:
Bangladesh faces a serious population problem characterized by high density, rapid growth in some areas, and uneven distribution. Limited land area combined with a large and growing population strains natural resources, housing, public services, and infrastructure, especially in cities like Dhaka where overcrowding fuels traffic congestion, pollution, and poor living conditions. High population pressure also worsens unemployment and underemployment, reduces per-capita access to healthcare and education, and increases vulnerability to disasters and food insecurity. Contributing factors include historically high fertility rates, rural-to-urban migration, early marriage, and limited awareness or access to family planning in some communities. Addressing the problem requires integrated policies: improving female education and employment opportunities, expanding family-planning services, investing in quality healthcare and reproductive education, and promoting sustainable urban planning and rural development to reduce migration pressure. Economic policies that create jobs outside major cities and strengthen agricultural productivity can ease resource stress. Environmental management and disaster preparedness are also essential, since climate impacts disproportionately affect densely populated, low-lying areas. With coordinated social, economic, and environmental strategies, Bangladesh can manage population pressures while improving living standards and sustainable development for its people.

[math]\textbf{Digital Bangladesh}[/math]

 The term “Digital Bangladesh” became popular after 2009 when the government announced it as a core objective. The goal is to make services easier, cheaper, and more accessible to the people through digital means.[math]\textbf{Achievements:}[/math]
 Bangladesh has made great progress. Most government services are now available online. Digital classrooms, online banking, mobile money, and apps have improved people's lives. The National ID system and e-passport are examples of digital tools that serve millions.[math]\textbf{Impact on Education and Economy:}[/math]

 Lack of internet access in rural areas, electricity problems, and cyber security risks are major challenges. Digital literacy is still low among the elderly and poor.[math]\textbf{Conclusion:}[/math]
 Digital Bangladesh is not just a dream, it is becoming a reality. With proper training, investment, and awareness, Bangladesh can become a strong digital economy.

Digital Bangladesh বিষয়ে সঠিক ২০০ শব্দের রচনা হওয়ার কারণ হলো এটি সংক্ষিপ্ত অথচ পূর্ণভাবে বিষয়ের সংজ্ঞা, ইতিহাস, লক্ষ্য ও অর্জনগুলো প্রদর্শন করে, ফলে পাঠক দ্রুত ধারণা पেতে পারে। মূল ভাবনা হলো তথ্য ও যোগাযোগ প্রযুক্তি দ্বারা কিভাবে সরকারের পরিষেবা, শিক্ষা, স্বচ্ছতা ও অর্থনীতিকে উন্নত করা যায়—এই কারিগরি ও সামাজিক প্রভাবগুলোকে উদাহরণসহ সংক্ষিপ্তভাবে তুলে ধরা রচনাটিকে কার্যকর করে। ২০০ শব্দের সীমা লেখাকে ফোকাসড রাখে এবং প্রাসঙ্গিক তথ্য ও উপযুক্ত উপসংহার দেওয়ার সুযোগ দেয়, যা পরীক্ষায় বা শিক্ষায় দরকারী সংক্ষিপ্ত ও স্পষ্ট ব্যাখ্যা নিশ্চিত করে।

Question #117 (ID: 578883)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Context: You are preparing a short 200-word composition titled "Life Along Bangladesh's Rivers" that captures daily life, economic roles, cultural significance, threats, and ways to protect rivers. After the composition, answer focused sub-questions about economic importance, threats with community solutions, and a brief concluding sentence.

Options:
a. Write the 200-word composition "Life Along Bangladesh's Rivers."
b. List five key points summarizing the rivers' economic importance.
c. Identify four major threats to rivers and propose one practical community-level solution for each threat.
d. Suggest a short concluding sentence (1–2 sentences) emphasizing river conservation.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
a Life Along Bangladesh's Rivers

Introduction: Rivers shape daily life across Bangladesh. Over seven hundred waterways wind through the land, bringing fertility, transport, and culture to millions. Farmers depend on seasonal floods that enrich soil with silt, enabling abundant rice and jute harvests. Fisherfolk launch boats before dawn, catching hilsa and dozens of freshwater species that feed families and support markets. Rivers serve as natural highways; passengers, goods, and traders travel by launches and country boats between villages and cities, knitting communities together.

Cultural and social life revolves around rivers. Festivals, folk songs, and boat races celebrate riverine heritage, while poets and painters draw inspiration from their shifting moods. Riverbanks host markets, schools, and mosques, forming lively centers of village life. Yet these waters face growing threats. Pollution from industry and homes, uncontrolled sand mining, and illegal encroachment reduce habitats and harm livelihoods. Climate change intensifies flooding and saline intrusion, challenging traditional practices.

Conclusion: Protecting rivers demands combined action: enforcing pollution controls, restoring wetlands, promoting sustainable fishing and river management, and empowering local communities to steward waterways. If preserved, Bangladesh’s rivers will continue to sustain life, culture, and prosperity for generations. Let future generations inherit clean, flowing rivers and protected shores.

b Five key economic points:
1. Agriculture: Rivers deposit fertile alluvial soil crucial for high rice and jute yields. 
2. Fisheries: Inland and estuarine fisheries (e.g., hilsa) provide food security and income for millions. 
3. Transport and trade: Waterways reduce transport costs and connect rural producers to urban markets. 
4. Livelihoods and employment: Boat-building, ferrying, fishing, and riverfront markets create numerous jobs. 
5. Ports and commerce: River ports and inland terminals support national and regional trade, lowering logistics costs.

c Four threats and community-level solutions:
1. Pollution (industrial and household waste) — Community solution: Organize local river-cleanup committees, set up community waste segregation and composting systems, and collaborate with local authorities to monitor and report illegal discharges.
2. Illegal river encroachment and land grabbing — Community solution: Form village vigilance groups that map and document riverbanks, publicly mark legal boundaries, and work with local government to enforce riparian rights.
3. Unsustainable sand mining — Community solution: Establish community-driven monitoring and reporting of mining sites, promote alternative local building materials, and petition for regulated, limited extraction zones with community oversight.
4. Overfishing and destructive fishing methods — Community solution: Create community fishing cooperatives that agree on seasonal no-take periods, ban destructive gear, and run awareness programs about sustainable yields.

d Short concluding sentence(s):
Protecting our rivers is protecting our future; communities must act now to restore and wisely manage waterways so they continue to sustain life, culture, and livelihoods.

Explanation:
Explanation:

a) Composition: The 200-word composition is structured to cover key aspects asked in the context—daily life, agriculture and fisheries, transport, cultural importance, threats, and needed actions. It uses concise paragraphs: introduction, cultural/social life, threats, and a call to action, ending with a brief final hope sentence to meet the requested length and focus.

b) Economic points: These five points highlight the main sectors through which rivers contribute to the economy—food production (agriculture, fisheries), movement of goods (transport), employment (local industries and services), and trade (ports). Each point is chosen because it has widespread, measurable impacts on livelihoods and GDP.

c) Threats and community solutions: The threats listed are common, tangible problems for Bangladeshi rivers: pollution, encroachment, sand mining, and overfishing. Community-level solutions are practical, low-cost, and empower local stakeholders—monitoring, cooperative management, alternative livelihoods or materials, and collaboration with authorities increase the likelihood of sustained improvements.

d) Concluding sentence: The suggested two-sentence conclusion is deliberately short and actionable: it links river protection to future wellbeing and emphasizes immediate community engagement and wise management, reinforcing themes in the composition.

Overall approach: The answers balance descriptive narrative (composition) with actionable, community-focused recommendations. Emphasis is on realistic measures communities can adopt alongside policy and enforcement to preserve riverine ecosystems and the services they provide.

Question:
You have been asked to produce a short composition and related brief tasks about Bangladesh. Use the context below to complete the sub-questions.

Context: Bangladesh is a nation of rivers, rich culture, resilient people, and growing development. Highlight its natural features, cultural life, and express a personal hope for its future in concise pieces.

Options:
a. Write a composition of exactly 200 words titled "Bangladesh: Land of Rivers and Resilience."
b. List five important geographical features of Bangladesh (one-line each).
c. Name three major festivals of Bangladesh and describe Pahela Baishakh in two sentences.
d. Write one concluding sentence expressing a personal aspiration for Bangladesh's future.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
a Bangladesh: Land of Rivers and Resilience

Bangladesh is my cherished homeland, a nation in South Asia renowned for its riverine landscapes and resilient people. Though small in size, it overflows with cultural richness, historical depth, and natural variety. The country earned independence in 1971 after a brave struggle, and its spirit of unity and perseverance continues to define the nation. Fertile plains fed by the Padma, Jamuna, and Meghna rivers sustain agriculture and shape daily life. The Sundarbans, a sprawling mangrove forest, shelters the majestic Bengal tiger and supports coastal ecosystems. Cox’s Bazar, with its long sandy shore, draws visitors from near and far.

Bangladeshi culture sparkles through music, literature, festivals, and cuisine. Bengalis celebrate Pahela Baishakh, Eid, and Durga Puja with colorful traditions, food, and communal joy. The garment industry, remittances, and an expanding technology sector fuel economic growth, while investments in education and health aim to improve living standards. Challenges like floods, poverty, and infrastructure strains persist, yet innovation and community solidarity drive progress. I am proud to be part of this land of rivers and resilience, and I hope to contribute to a future where every citizen thrives and Bangladesh’s beauty and strength shine on world stage.

b 1. The deltaic plains formed by the Padma, Jamuna, and Meghna rivers — fertile and densely populated.
2. The Sundarbans mangrove forest — the largest of its kind, home to the Bengal tiger.
3. Cox’s Bazar coastline — the world’s longest natural sea beach.
4. Hill tracts in the southeast — hilly, forested regions with indigenous communities.
5. Numerous inland wetlands (haors and beels) — important for fisheries and seasonal ecology.

c Major festivals: Pahela Baishakh, Eid-ul-Fitr (Eid), Durga Puja.
Pahela Baishakh is the Bengali New Year celebrated on the first day of the Bengali calendar with colorful processions, music, traditional dress, and communal feasting. It symbolizes cultural renewal and unity, as people of all ages join street fairs, performances, and heartfelt greetings.

d I aspire to contribute my skills so that Bangladesh becomes a prosperous, climate-resilient nation where every child receives quality education and every family enjoys secure livelihoods.

Explanation:
The solution provides a 200-word composition (count verified) focused on Bangladesh’s geography, culture, history, economy, and a hopeful personal note. Sub-question (b) lists five concise geographic features chosen for their significance to Bangladesh’s environment, biodiversity, and human settlement. Sub-question (c) names three widely observed festivals and gives a two-sentence description of Pahela Baishakh emphasizing its cultural importance and typical activities. Sub-question (d) offers a single, forward-looking sentence expressing a personal aspiration aligned with development and resilience themes. The composition structure uses an introduction, key details (geography and culture), development context, challenges, and a concluding personal hope to meet typical composition requirements.

Question #120 (ID: 578841)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Your final exams are only two weeks away, and you realize your Bangla paper, especially literature and grammar, needs urgent work. You decide to write an e-mail to a senior classmate who always excels in Bangla to request specific help and to arrange a short study meet-up.

Options:
a. Write the e-mail to your senior asking for help (include subject, salutation, body and closing).
b. List the key Bangla poems, prose pieces, and writing formats you should prioritise for revision.
c. Give three clear grammar tips with a common mistake and its correction for each tip.
d. Propose a polite plan for a one-hour study session (date, time, place, agenda) and write a brief follow-up line asking for confirmation.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
a
To: tanvir.senior@example.com

Subject: Request for urgent Bangla guidance and study session

Dear Tanvir,

I hope you are doing well. Our final exams are just two weeks away and I am quite worried about the Bangla paper. I have not been able to prepare the literature and grammar parts properly. Since you always do very well in Bangla, I would be extremely grateful if you could help me out.

Could you please send me:
1) A short list of the most important poems, prose passages and novels/short stories to revise.  
2) Any sample essays or formats you recommend (and a brief outline or model answer if possible).  
3) Key grammar tips and common mistakes to watch for.  
4) Any past questions or notes you have.

If you are available, would you be willing to meet for a 1-hour study session this coming Saturday at 4:00 pm at the library near our college? I think going over summaries and doing a few practice questions together would help a lot.

Thank you so much for your time and help. Please let me know what works for you.

With thanks,

Arif

b
Prioritised list for quick revision:
- Poems: 1) "Bidrohi" (Kazi Nazrul Islam) — themes & imagery; 2) Selected Tagore poems (e.g., "Ekla Cholo Re") — message and poetic devices; 3) Jasimuddin’s folk-style poems — rural imagery.
- Prose/Short stories & Novels: 1) "Pather Panchali" (Bibhutibhushan Bandopadhyay) — main plot and characters; 2) "Lalsalu"/"Tree without Leaves" (Syed Waliullah) — themes and symbolism; 3) Representative short stories by Rabindranath Tagore and contemporary Bangladeshi writers — plot and moral.
- Essays & Formats: 1) Familiar essay topics (education, environment, youth and patriotism) with one-paragraph outlines; 2) Formal letter format (application/complaint) and informal letter; 3) Summary writing and comprehension techniques.
- Language skills: comprehension strategies, paraphrasing, vocabulary often used in exams.

c
Three grammar tips with common mistakes and corrections:
1) Tense consistency:
   - Mistake: "Yesterday he goes to the market and buys fruits."  
   - Correction: "Yesterday he went to the market and bought fruits."  
   - Tip: Keep past narration in past tense throughout unless there is a reason to change tense.
2) Subject-verb agreement:
   - Mistake: "The group of students are ready."  
   - Correction: "The group of students is ready."  
   - Tip: Identify the main subject (group) rather than nearby plural noun (students).
3) Proper use of conjunctions and punctuation:
   - Mistake: "I wanted to study but I was tired I could not concentrate."  
   - Correction: "I wanted to study, but I was tired, so I could not concentrate."  
   - Tip: Use commas before conjunctions joining independent clauses and insert connecting words where needed.

d
Proposed study session plan and follow-up line:
- Date & Time: Saturday (two days from now), 4:00 pm – 5:00 pm.
- Place: College library, Study Room B (quiet corner near the windows).
- Agenda (one hour): 1) 15 minutes — quick rundown of the prioritized poem/prose list; 2) 20 minutes — review 1 model essay outline and one sample formal letter; 3) 20 minutes — practice 2 short comprehension questions and discuss grammar tips; 4) 5 minutes — decide follow-up tasks.
- Materials to bring: notes, any past questions, pens and a notebook.

Follow-up confirmation line to include in the e-mail: "Would Saturday at 4:00 pm at the college library suit you? Please let me know if another time is better. Thank you!"


Explanation:
Reasoning behind the solution:
- Part (a): The sample e-mail follows a polite, concise structure: subject line, greeting, clear requests (specific items the senior can provide), a meeting suggestion, gratitude, and a sign-off. Asking for specific items (list of works, sample answers, grammar tips, past questions) helps the friend respond quickly and usefully.
- Part (b): The prioritized list focuses on items commonly tested in Bangla exams: key poems, representative prose and novels, and practical writing formats. It balances content knowledge (authors, themes) with exam skills (essay formats, summaries).
- Part (c): Grammar tips are chosen because tense errors, subject-verb agreement, and punctuation/conjunction mistakes are frequent and easy to improve quickly. Each tip includes a typical incorrect sentence and a corrected version so the student can see the rule applied.
- Part (d): A one-hour session plan is realistic and focused: short segments on revision, practice, and planning further study make the meeting effective. The follow-up line is polite and asks for confirmation while offering flexibility.

Overall, the solution aims to provide the student with a ready-to-send e-mail, concrete revision targets, practical grammar fixes, and a clear, short study plan — all designed for quick, high-impact exam preparation.

Question:
You are preparing a short composition about your very first morning at a new school. Describe the events, your feelings, the people you met, and how the day changed you. In addition to the composition, complete three brief related tasks about word choice and the lesson you learned.

Options:
a. Write a composition titled "My First Morning at the New School" in about 200 words.
b. Give a five-word descriptive subtitle for your composition.
c. List five vivid words from the composition that convey feelings or atmosphere.
d. Write one-sentence moral or lesson you learned from that day.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
a My First Morning at the New School

The memory of my first morning at the new school remains vivid. I walked through the iron gates feeling nervous and small, my bright bag feeling heavier than it looked. The playground buzzed with voices; flags fluttered and a row of colorful banners welcomed the students. A kind teacher with a warm smile guided me to my classroom, and her gentle voice made the unfamiliar place feel less intimidating. I was eager to explore: the books smelled of ink, the blackboard held neatly written alphabets, and the desks were arranged in neat rows facing the window. Beside me sat a boy who introduced himself and shared his sandwich; his friendliness turned my anxiety into curiosity. During the morning assembly we sang together, and each chorus stitched me more tightly into the school’s rhythm. Small routines—lining up, raising hands, repeating rhymes—began to build my confidence. Though I fumbled with names and dropped my pencil, classmates helped me without mockery. By the time the bell rang, the school that had seemed enormous in the morning now felt like a community where I might belong. I left with a light step and a promise to return the next day with a braver heart.

b Nervous Beginnings, Friendly Faces, Hopeful

c nervous; eager; colorful; curiosity; comforting

d Lesson: Small acts of kindness can turn fear into belonging and help you grow more confident.

Explanation:

Word choice: I intentionally used sensory and emotional words (e.g., "nervous," "colorful," "eager") to convey atmosphere and internal state. The five-word subtitle compresses the main emotional arc: initial nervousness, meeting friendly faces, and hopeful outlook. The five vivid words listed in part (c) were chosen because they appear in the composition and directly signal emotion or setting: "nervous" conveys initial anxiety, "eager" shows readiness to explore, "colorful" evokes cheerful visual detail, "curiosity" captures the shift from fear to interest, and "comforting" (implied by the teacher's warm smile) summarizes the supportive tone. The one-sentence moral summarizes the central takeaway: supportive people and small routines help a newcomer feel welcome and confident. The composition was kept to about 200 words to meet the task requirement and to practice concise, vivid storytelling.

Question:
You are asked to prepare a short composition and related tasks on the theme of teenage substance abuse for a school awareness folder. Produce a 200-word composition and answer the accompanying items below.
